Military Police Conflict in Wuchang 125

The garrison brigade and security regiment exchanged gunfire

One pedestrian killed and several injured

A dispatch from Hankou reports that a conflict occurred in Shouyi Park, Wuchang, on the 25th of this month between the Hubei garrison brigade and the security regiment. Both sides exchanged gunfire, killing one pedestrian and injuring several others. The circumstances of the incident are as follows: the garrison brigade was stationed at Xindi and recently received orders to return to Wuhan. Brigade Commander Rong Jingfang led the troops. On the 24th, most of the troops had arrived and were stationed at Majubuju, the Ordnance Bureau, and other places. At 4:00 PM that afternoon, the 5th and 8th companies of the 2nd regiment of the brigade were watching a play at the Shouyi Park theater when a dispute occurred with the 7th company of the security regiment, which was responsible for guarding the park. The dispute soon dispersed. However, at 1:00 PM on the 25th, Liu Yushan, the attached company commander of the 7th company of the security regiment, led 16 armed soldiers and one squad leader to the theater to maintain order. Many soldiers from the 5th company of the garrison brigade also arrived, and the two sides clashed, causing great disorder. Company Commander Liu immediately telegraphed the regimental headquarters to dispatch more than 20 armed soldiers from the 7th company, led by Deputy Regiment Commander Wu Changxu, to suppress the situation from the top of the park mountain at Doujiying. However, dozens of soldiers from the 6th company of the 2nd regiment of the garrison brigade also arrived. Gunfire erupted, and the situation became extremely tense. An elderly woman surnamed Liu was killed, and three civilians were injured. Afterward, the security regiment reported to the provincial government and the garrison headquarters, stating that "the garrison brigade seized two Type 79 rifles from the regiment's patrol team, damaged one, and the regiment also captured nine garrison brigade soldiers on the spot: He Kunshan, Yang Shuming, Meng Wenqi, Chen Zhanbiao, Xu Yulin, Xiang Junbo, Guan Honghua, He Liang, Lin Yishu, Lian Deng, and nine rank badges, seven armbands, six bullets, and one grenade base, which were collected by the regimental headquarters. In addition, the 9th company of the regiment, stationed at the Pinghu Gate and Shouyi Park, had more than 20 rifles confiscated and more than ten soldiers captured by the garrison brigade troops, and they also dispatched troops to guard the Hanyang Gate area," etc. Wu Muni, the chairman of the recreation ground's board of directors, also reported the incident to the Wuchang Garrison District Commander for investigation. It is reported that Director He was very angry about the incident and decided to thoroughly investigate the situation and severely punish the perpetrators. The Garrison Command has also sent personnel to conduct a thorough investigation for reporting purposes (25th).

Shang Zhen and Xu Yongchang Go to Beiping to Visit Zhang Zuolin to Handle Post-War Matters in Shanxi 126

Rong Honglu Discusses the Results of His Trip to Shenyang

Taiyuan Dispatch: The post-war situation in Shanxi has not made much progress. Some generals recently went to Shenyang together to appeal for military funds. Shang Zhen and Xu Yongchang recently went to Beiping to visit Zhang Zuolin for assistance. The future of Shanxi depends greatly on this trip by Shang and Xu. According to Shang and Xu's pre-departure statements, they seem to have great determination regarding military expenditures this time. If military funds are not secured for even one day, the people of Shanxi will have to bear the burden of supplying the military. Other extractions and the invisible losses to the people are even more difficult to calculate. Since Yan Xishan left Shanxi, each county in southern and eastern Shanxi has provided military expenses ranging from more than one million to at least four or five hundred thousand. The suffering of the people can be imagined.

Rong Honglu, who went to Shenyang to visit Zhang Zuolin, returned to Taiyuan yesterday. According to his remarks, he visited Zhang four times before and after his arrival in Shenyang. Zhang left Fengtian (Shenyang) for Tianjin. Zhang said that the post-war settlement in Shanxi regarding military pay of one million to cover demobilization costs is now no longer a problem. Once all the procedures are completed, the money can be allocated. Regarding other pay, Zhang has expressed his sincere intention verbally and is actively planning. Although it is impossible to say when the money will be allocated, observing Zhang's attitude, it is entirely possible to raise it. Zhang is also very concerned about financial matters, but Zhang himself has no specific proposals on how to handle them. The most he can do is appeal to the central government to restore public bonds. Zhang has directly interceded with the central government to alleviate the situation. All the systems of the Garrison Department will be directly under the Deputy Commander-in-Chief. However, for the sake of facilitating contact, he will consult with the provincial government when necessary to carry out everything. Although the organizational content is not yet determined, it is generally not much different from the Garrison Headquarters. As for the Garrison Division, it is internally divided into two brigades and six regiments. The selection of personnel has not yet been decided.

Wang Jingguo said that since the reorganization of the Jin-Sui Army, in order for the army commanders to report the reorganization process to Deputy Commander Zhang after the inspections by the Central Government and the Northeast, Commander Sun Cuiai, Artillery Supervisor Zhou Dai, Division Commander Feng Pengzhu, Division Commander Li Muyan, and Division Commander Yang Yaofang went to Shenyang to visit the Deputy Commander. It is speculated by outsiders that they went to the Deputy Commander to request reorganization fees and military expenses, but this is just conjecture by outsiders because Commander Sun, Division Commanders Feng and Li are responsible for military expenses and reorganization fees. Commanders Sun, Feng and Li recently telegraphed that they had left Shenyang and started their journey back to Shanxi on Hao Chen (date not specified). It is estimated that they will arrive in Beiping yesterday (20th). Once Chairman Shang and Military Commander Xu arrive in Beiping, Sun, Feng, Li, Yang and Zhou will be able to return to Shanxi. Military Commander Xu also started from Taiyuan this noon. The date for Division Commander Li Shengda, Division Commander Yang Xiaoou and his brothers (Wang's self-designation) to go to Beiping will be determined after Sun, Feng, Li, and Yang return. Army Commander Yang Chengyuan will postpone his departure due to defense issues. Army Commander Yang Ai Yuan will not be able to leave Taiyuan because he is in charge of Shanxi's military affairs. In the future, after Chairman Shang or Military Commander Xu return, Yang will be able to go to Beiping. Currently, the issues we most hope to resolve are military expenses and finances. This visit to the Deputy Commander by Shang and Xu should allow them to request specific solutions to these issues (22nd).

National Elections in Shanxi Province Completed 127

Forty-Seven Cities and Counties Qualified to Elect

Taiyuan Dispatch: In Shanxi Province, apart from the party member elections in 13 counties, which the provincial party headquarters has telegraphed to limit reporting by the 23rd of this month, registration of people's organizations in other counties and cities ended uniformly at 12:00 PM the day before yesterday (20th). However, the elections in Yangcheng, Qinshui, Lingchuan, Yuxiang, and Sixian did not arrive on schedule and have been declared invalid. According to statistics, a total of 97 cities and counties out of 108 cities and counties in Shanxi Province submitted voter lists. After review, only 51 cities and counties were deemed qualified. Now, excluding the four counties of Qinshui, only 47 cities and counties actually participated. A total of more than 130,000 ballots were issued. Based on the total population of 13 million in the province, approximately one in every hundred people obtained the right to vote. The election results office completed the statistics last night, but for the sake of prudence, it is planned to formally announce the results after a second review. It is reported that the Provincial Party Headquarters has decided on the executive committee members for the party member elections: Han Kewen and Hu Biyue. Among others in the education sector and people's liberal professional organizations, Wang Luxun, president of Shanxi University, and Su Tiren are the most promising. In agricultural associations, Liu Kuijiu, president of the Agricultural College, and Wu Zhenduo and Zhao Xuan are the most promising. In chambers of commerce, Wang Xian and Song Chunru are the most promising. The provincial office has already prepared matters concerning the representatives going to Beijing. The Provincial Party Headquarters and various people's organizations have jointly established a National Assembly Propaganda Committee, which will hold a National Assembly Propaganda Week from May 1st to 7th and hold a celebration rally on the opening day of the National Assembly. The preparatory committee is actively preparing (April 22nd).

Severe Flooding in the Han River in Eastern Guangdong 128

Many Dikes Below Chaoan Have Collapsed

Shantou Dispatch: The mountains east of the Dayu Ridge on the border of Guangdong and Jiangxi rapidly approach northern Fujian and connect with the Thirty-Six Peaks of Mount Wuyi. All the waters north and east of this ridge converge at Sanheba in Dapu, forming the Han River. The Han River flows through Fengshun and Chaoan from Sanhe, then splits into several branches that run through Jieyang and Chenghai counties, exiting into the sea. The Han River, from Sanhe downstream to above Chaoan City for more than 200 li, becomes a single channel with a large flow. Both banks are high mountains composed of yellow soil, with pine and bamboo widely planted on the mountains, forming natural forest farms. The yellow soil is eroded by the water year by year, flowing down below Chaoan City and accumulating in the riverbed. The riverbed gradually becomes higher than the plains. Chenghai counties are all plains, the most fertile and the richest in agricultural products. Since the riverbed is high and there are no barren mountains on both sides, the farmers built dikes to protect against the water. The north dike is more than 30 feet above the ground, extending from outside the north gate of Chaoan to Yixi Station, about 4 li long. If the Han River water is higher than the dike or unfortunately collapses, the Chaojie area will become a swamp. This year, since the beginning of spring, it has been raining continuously, with no sunshine for hundreds of days. Mountain water on the border of Fujian and Jiangxi erupted and rushed to the Han River, flowing to the sea. On the 16th, the Han River water was vast, carrying yellow mud and fences downstream. On the 18th, the east, south, and north gates of Chaoan City were all flooded, with the east gate being the most severely flooded. Thirteen wooden boards were quickly lowered to the gate to block the water. Steamships and sailboats stopped running due to the rapid current and were docked outside the Shangshui Gate Bamboo Wood Gate, with mooring ropes tied to the battlements of the city wall. From the boats, the city could be looked down upon. The water level downstream of the Han River rose eight or nine feet, directly impacting the dikes of Chenghai. Yuzhou, Outing, Dongdun, and Fulong all became swamps, and agricultural crops were severely damaged. The Shantou-Chenghai Road has been closed since the 16th, and electric ferries to Chenghai have also been suspended due to the rapid water. On the 19th, more than 100 zhang of the Xiapu Bridge on the Shantou-Chenghai Road, Chenghai shore, was washed away by the water. Sections of the Chaozhou-Shantou Railway below Anbu, Yuepu, Qishan, and Xinxiang were submerged in a sea of water. At the Huawu and Huilan bridges in Shantou, where the river water flows into the sea, the water roared like thunder and ten thousand horses galloping. Two salt boats were swept away by the water, losing about 3,000 dan of salt.

On the 20th and 21st, haze filled the air and the rain did not stop. The sad and miserable atmosphere filled the world. The Chaoan North Dike was already in a dangerous state. The Han River roared, and the waves rose and fell. Chaoan County Magistrate Ruan personally inspected the North Dike and prepared iron bars, fir wood, and workers to prevent any unforeseen circumstances. On the 21st, various charitable halls and the detective team leader in Chaoan guarded the north and south dikes. Huang Jianjin was responsible for the North Dike, and Ke Mao Zhang was responsible for the South Dike, with three police officers overseeing. On the night of the 21st, the dikes in the Jiangqu and Jianggui districts sent out emergency warnings that water was penetrating the culverts and flooding the entire township. More than 3,000 able-bodied men rushed to the rescue, fortunately averting disaster. The East Gate had already lowered 14 boards, with water filling nine boards. On the opposite bank, more than ten zhang of the Dongjin Dike were washed away, and there were many leaks in the north and south dikes. Coal gas lamps were lit in many places on both dikes, and the able-bodied men of each township braved the rain, sitting on the banks to guard. The Longhou Dike in Chenghai collapsed, and the fields were a sea of water. The major dikes of Donghupu and Mei also overflowed. Chenghai County Magistrate Huang Guoliang supervised thousands of civilians to guard them. As of noon today (22nd), the rain had not stopped and the thunder rumbled, the sky was as dark as lacquer, and it is unknown how the dike guards were suffering in the rain (22nd).

Airplane Show at the Aviation Conference 129

The secretariat of the Aviation Conference, in order to increase the aviation interest of members and the public, invited Chinese and foreign aviators to perform flying techniques at the Ming Palace airfield from 9:00 AM to 12:00 PM yesterday, and Deputy Captain Ding Jixu of the Sixth Aviation Team jumped with an insurance umbrella. Notices were issued to various organizations, groups, and schools in advance, and advertisements were published to invite people from all walks of life to visit. Yesterday, about a thousand people from all walks of life went to visit. The main entrance of the airfield, which is usually prohibited from passing, was specially opened yesterday. Inside and outside the gate were covered with various colored slogans. Dozens of airplanes were arranged along the east side of the airfield. The viewing areas for guests, members, and groups were marked separately with white chalk lines, and the public was in the southeastern corner, with officers and aviation class students divided into shifts to direct and entertain, and the order was well maintained. First, aviation class instructors Shi Mansheng and Li Ruibin and one student each drove Morse aircraft and took off one after another, scattering colored leaflets from the air, which fell all over the airfield. The leaflets were printed with various slogans of the Aviation Conference, and the crowds scrambled to pick them up. Soon after, the three Morse aircraft landed one after another. Immediately, Ding Jixu, the attached captain of the Sixth Aviation Team, alone drove a high-powered Cossack fighter plane into the air, circling the field once, then opening the throttle to perform stunts. First, he made a small turn, during which the fuselage was sideways in the air. Next, he made a somersault, with the fuselage flipping upwards, going around to the rear. Next, he made a "tearing split" (Slsiu), with the fuselage standing upside down in the air and the wings circling around the fuselage like a windmill, causing the audience to gasp in amazement. After a while, Yan Yucong, the captain of the First Aviation Team, and Mao Bangchu, the chief flying instructor of the Aviation Class, also drove similar Cossack aircraft into the air, performing formation flying together with Ding Jixu's aircraft. The three aircraft were very close to each other, flying in a wedge formation, resembling a flock of geese. Next, British aviators Xiawei and Xie Erjun successively drove British aircraft, Yaviang and Flitidy, into the air, each performing stunts, each doing their best. Next, American aviators Anlisheng and Fu Ang drove Fei Erkang and Funajilin aircraft to form a formation flight, their formation changes were extremely agile. Next, they each performed stunts separately before landing. Finally, German aviator Li Cider drove a Junkers A47 aircraft, this aircraft had the largest horsepower and the loudest sound. It was an all-metal low-wing, twin-rudder aircraft in sea green color, shaped extremely strong. Mr. Li has performed many times in Beijing, and his performances are amazing to watch. Yesterday's performance was even more outstanding, such as not ascending against the wind, but deliberately ascending with the wind, and suddenly turning the fuselage upwards when running from the starting point to three or four hundred meters. Also, the "tearing split" he performed was the most urgent and the most numerous. The low-altitude flights skimmed over people's heads several times, and the fuselage was arbitrarily flipped left and right, straight up and down in the air, making all kinds of dangerous situations that made people gasp in amazement. After the stunt flying performance was over, Attached Team Captain Ding Jixu performed the insurance umbrella jump. Chief Instructor Mao Bangchu and Ding drove the Cossack aircraft into the air and gradually turned to the sky just north of Hongwu Gate. At this time, the height of the aircraft was more than 3,000 feet. Suddenly, Ding was seen like a black dot detaching from the aircraft and falling. After about three seconds, the insurance umbrella opened leisurely and slowly drifted in the wind for about six or seven minutes, safely landing in the wheat field at the foot of the city wall. For a time, the crowd cheered, all admiring Ding's excellent technique and his bravery. It is reported that Zhang Huichang, the director of the Aviation Administration, has specially added one month's salary to Ding to express his encouragement.

Jiangsu Provincial Government Plans to Open a New Port at Xiangshan 130

Restore and Prosper the Industrial and Commercial Center of the Provincial Capital

Zhenjiang was once an important town of Jingkou and is now the capital of Jiangsu Province. Last year, its population exceeded 180,000. It is located at the crossroads of land and water transportation, with favorable transportation conditions. Industry and commerce once flourished extremely. However, since the shift of canal transport to sea transport and the completion of the Jinpu Railway, the transportation center has moved accordingly. In recent years, the original wharves have been severely affected by sandbars, and ships cannot dock, causing the industry and commerce to decline sharply. When the provincial government moved to Zhenjiang two years ago, the Water Conservancy Bureau measured the area of Zheng Runzhou and the depth of the Yangtze River, planning to remedy the old wharf. However, the plan failed to proceed due to the bureau's instability and lack of funds. Subsequently, the Provincial Water Conservancy Bureau measured the water depth and terrain of the Jiang River bank between Xiangshan and Beigushan and compared it with the maps produced by the customs over the years, and decided to build a new port at Xiangshan in Zhenjiang and open a new market in order to restore and prosper the industry and commerce of the provincial capital. The detailed plan has been submitted by the Construction Department and passed by the Provincial Government's 391st meeting last week, and work has begun. The following is a summary of the new port plan:

(A) Port Area 131

East from Xiangshan to Dajiaochang, north to the deep Hong of the Yangtze River, and south to Huashan as a barrier, the area has a total area of about three square kilometers. To sum up, its advantages in design are six: (1) This area is flat arable land connected to the old city market and is very close to the South Gate Station of the Beijing-Shanghai Railway, which can be used to build cargo lines directly to the pier. (2) The ground is vast and can reap the benefits of flat land construction. (3) A large amount of land can be pre-emptively acquired at a low price for public buildings such as roads, ports, rivers, ponds, and warehouses. (4) The design can be comprehensively planned, and the construction can be implemented in stages. (5) The roads in the area are easy to connect with the old city. (6) In the future, the urban area will prosper, and it can develop south to the South Railway Station and east even more broadly.

(B) Overview of Equipment 132

(Zi) The urban area has a total area of ​​more than three square kilometers. It is estimated that it can be divided into three parts: more than 10,000 acres are allocated to public piers and commercial areas, that is, the central and western parts of the area; more than 4,800 acres are allocated to industrial areas, that is, the eastern part of the area; and more than 15,400 acres are allocated as forest garden residential areas, that is, the mountainous areas around Huashan and Beigushan. (Chou) Wharf construction is divided into lighter boats, river boats, boat ponds, railways, and cargo depots. (Yin) A branch line is built from the Zhenjiang South Gate Station of the Beijing-Shanghai Line, crossing Huashan and reaching the Jiang River bank pier, and another branch line runs along the Jiang River Avenue and the river bank of the boat river. Both end at the western end of the boat river. (Mao) The roads use crushed stone as the road surface. Its three main lines connecting the outside of the area connect with the Jiang River Avenue in the old city via the waist of Beigushan Mountain, and one connects with Zhongzheng Road in the city via the mountain depression of Beigushan Beicheng, directly reaching the Grand Market, and one connects directly to Beimen and Zhongshan Road in the city. The road width is 18 meters. With these three main lines, none of the main avenues in the old city are not connected to the roads in the new city, that is, there are convenient connections everywhere between the old and new areas. (Chen) The cargo depot is a one-story warehouse building with a total area of ​​28,000 square meters. If the average volume of each cubic meter is one ton, the applicable volume of the cargo depot can store 50,000 tons of cargo at the same time. Even if the total tonnage of cargo entering and leaving the port annually is around 5 million tons, it can be handled with ease.

(C) Project Expenses 133

(1) The estimated cost of the urban area filling project is 364,000 yuan. (2) The estimated cost of the wharf project is 596,490 yuan. (3) The estimated cost of the road project is 284,512 yuan. (4) The estimated cost of the cargo depot construction is 364,000 yuan. The total cost of the four items is 1,609,000 yuan, all of which will be allocated from the construction public bonds. The construction costs of the railway and railway bridges should belong to the railway bureau and are not included.

Public Official Appointment Law Already Passed 134

The Public Official Appointment Law has now been amended and passed by the Legislative Yuan at its 141st meeting on the 25th. The full text is recorded as follows: (Article 1) The appointment of public officials shall be governed by this law, unless otherwise provided by law. (Article 2) A public official in the Selected Appointment rank shall be appointed from among those who possess one of the following qualifications: 1. Currently serving or having served in a Selected Appointment position and having passed a screening and examination or performance appraisal; 2. Currently serving or having served in the highest Recommended Appointment position for two years or more and having passed a screening and examination or performance appraisal; 3. Having served as an education official for one year or more; 4. Having rendered special meritorious service to the Republic of China or having devoted oneself to the National Revolution for ten years or more and having rendered meritorious service; 5. Having special writings or inventions in academics. (Article 3) A public official in the Recommended Appointment rank shall be appointed from among those who possess one of the following qualifications: 1. Having passed the Higher Examination or a special examination equivalent to the Higher Examination; 2. Currently serving or having served in a Recommended Appointment position and having passed a screening and examination or performance appraisal; 3. Currently serving or having served in the highest Delegated Appointment position for three years or more and having passed a screening and examination or performance appraisal; 4. Having rendered meritorious service to the Republic of China or having devoted oneself to the National Revolution for seven years or more and having achieved results; 5. Having graduated from a domestic or foreign university recognized by the Ministry of Education and having specialized writings that have passed examination. (Article 4) A public official in the Delegated Appointment rank shall be appointed from among those who possess one of the following qualifications:

Page 10

1. Having passed the Ordinary Examination or a special examination equivalent to the Ordinary Examination; 2. Currently serving or having served in a Delegated Appointment position and having passed a screening and examination or performance appraisal; 3. Currently employed as a staff member and having continued to serve for three years or more with excellent performance; 4. Having devoted oneself to the National Revolution for five years or more and having achieved results; 5. Having graduated from a specialized school or above. (Article 5) In addition to the provisions of the preceding three articles, the appointment of public officials shall be limited to those whose academic knowledge and experience are commensurate with the duties of the position to be held. (Article 6) A person who has one of the following circumstances shall not be appointed as a public official: 1. Having been deprived of civil rights and not yet restored; 2. Having embezzled public funds and not yet repaid; 3. Having been punished for corruption; 4. Using opium or its substitutes. (Article 7) The appointment of public officials in the Selected Appointment and Recommended Appointment ranks shall be submitted by the National Government to the Ministry of Personnel for examination and approval, and then appointed separately. The appointment of public officials in the Delegated Appointment rank shall be submitted by the responsible official to the Ministry of Personnel for examination and approval, and then delegated. The Ministry of Personnel shall immediately conduct an examination to determine whether it is qualified or unqualified upon receiving the aforementioned two documents. (Article 8) During the period of requesting Selected Appointment, presenting Recommended Appointment, or proposing Delegated Appointment, the responsible official may, when necessary, appoint a person with appropriate qualifications as an agent, but the period of agency shall not exceed three months. (Article 9) Persons who have passed the examination shall be assigned to relevant government offices for appointment according to the type and subject of the examination. (Article 10) Public officials in the Recommended Appointment and Delegated Appointment ranks shall be given priority in appointment to those who have passed the examination. The appointment of persons who have passed the examination shall be in the order of distribution by the Ministry of Personnel. (Article 11) The appointment procedure is divided into probationary appointment and substantive appointment. A person who has completed one year of probationary appointment may be granted substantive appointment. (Article 12) Newly appointed personnel shall be on probationary appointment and shall be appointed from the lowest salary grade. However, those who have served as public officials and have accumulated seniority and meritorious service may be appointed to their original grade. Those who have the qualifications for Selected Appointment but are appointed to Recommended Appointment, or those who have the qualifications for Recommended Appointment but are appointed to Delegated Appointment, may not be subject to the provisions of the preceding paragraph and may retain their original qualifications. (Article 13) This law shall not apply to political appointees. (Article 14) In order to implement this law, the Ministry of Personnel may separately draft regulations and submit them to the Examination Yuan for referral to the National Government for approval. (Article 15) The date of implementation of this law shall be determined by order.

Organizational Regulations for Establishment Bureau 135

The Legislative Yuan has amended and passed it.

The Legislative Yuan passed the Organizational Regulations for Establishment Bureau at its 141st meeting on the 25th as follows: (Article 1) In places where county governance has not yet been established in various provinces, an Establishment Bureau may be temporarily established in accordance with the provisions of these Regulations. At an appropriate time, county governance should be established. The abolition and establishment of the Establishment Bureau and the demarcation of its area shall be proposed by the provincial government in the form of maps and explanations, and submitted to the Ministry of Interior for referral to the Executive Yuan for submission to the National Government for approval and promulgation. (Article 3) The Establishment Bureau shall have one director who shall be under the command and supervision of the provincial government and handle administrative affairs within the jurisdiction. (Article 4) Within the scope of laws and regulations of the central government and the province, the Establishment Bureau may issue bureau orders and formulate separate rules. The aforementioned separate rules and important bureau orders shall be reported to the provincial government for verification and record. (Article 5) The director of the Establishment Bureau shall receive Recommended Appointment treatment. The Department of Civil Affairs shall propose personnel with the qualifications of a public official in the Recommended Appointment rank, which shall be decided by the provincial government for appointment and reported to the Ministry of Interior for record. However, in special circumstances, personnel with the following qualifications may be appointed: (1) A citizen of the Republic of China who is thirty years of age or older; (2) Graduated from a secondary school or above or has been engaged in administrative affairs for three years or more; (3) Understands Party principles; (4) Familiar with local conditions. (Article 6) The Establishment Bureau shall have assistant staff. The number and method of appointment shall be proposed by the Department of Civil Affairs and submitted to the provincial government for approval and reported to the Ministry of Interior for record. The Establishment Bureau may employ staff as appropriate. (Article 7) The administrative expenses of the Establishment Bureau shall be paid by the provincial treasury, but when necessary, the provincial government may consult with the Ministry of Interior and the Ministry of Finance for joint review and approval to be subsidized by the national treasury. (Article 8) The official seal of the Establishment Bureau shall be made by the Ministry of Interior according to the style and distributed by the provincial government. (Article 9) The Ministry of Interior shall determine the measures for promoting autonomy in the area under the jurisdiction of the Establishment Bureau. (Article 10) These Regulations shall be implemented from the date of promulgation.

Wanted Bandit Lu Yaosheng Arrested and Interrogated 138

After the bandit leaders Xu Tianxiong, Wang Qiming, and Xu Fusheng were arrested and executed, the people felt happy. However, it was heard that secondary leaders such as Lu Yaosheng and Yang Meimei continued to gather the remaining bandits in Taihu Lake. Cao Pang, the commander of the bandit suppression in the four counties of Songjiang, Jinshan, Jiading, and Pinghu, strictly ordered the subordinate land and water military police to arrest them by name in order to eradicate them completely and printed the wanted list. Today, it is widely rumored that Lu Yaosheng, the captain under Xu Tianxiong, was captured in Shanghai and will be escorted to the headquarters for interrogation.

Township Inspection Inspector to 139

Hu Gui, the inspector of the Provincial Township Clearing General Bureau, came to Songjiang and attached great importance to the defense corps in each district. Mr. Hu went to Fengjing today to inspect the defense corps in that district and investigate everything. He will also inspect Sijing, Tianmashan, and Xinzhuang.

Results of the Re-election of the First District Party Department Announced 140

With the approval of the County Party Rectification Committee, the re-election of the First District Party Department was held on the 26th. As a result of the election, Wu Guoxiu, Wang Zuyu, and Wang Lu were elected as executive committee members, and Hu Qi was elected as a supervisory committee member. The County Party Rectification Committee sent Ye Guanqun to supervise the election.

Suzhou

Elder Brother Heartlessly Strangles Younger Brother 141

A male corpse, already decomposed, was found in the river outside Guanmiao Lane a few days ago. The head was covered with a purse and the body was tied with a rope. After the court sent personnel to examine it, it was buried in a coffin. Subsequently, the detective team found out that the deceased's name was Gu Gengtu and he was killed by his elder brother Gu Jinshou. Gu Jinshou was arrested and confessed that the deceased was indeed his younger brother. Because he had forcibly borrowed money from him last winter, he harbored resentment. That night, he stayed at home and strangled Gengtu with a rope while he was asleep at midnight and dumped the body in the river. Yesterday, the murderer Gu Jinshou was escorted by the Public Security Bureau to the local court for interrogation.

Wuxi

Bandit Captured on Train Escorted to Beijing for Interrogation 142

The 26th slow train on the Beijing-Shanghai Railway, Beijing-Wuxi section, was passing Xiaoshan at 6:00 p.m. on the 21st of this month when Inspector Zhang Hong, who was traveling with the train, together with the military police on the train, shot and killed Zhang Jianxun, a bandit with a gun, in the carriage and captured three bandits, Zhang Erlou, Kai Zao, and Chen Shikui, who were escorted to the 4th Regiment headquarters in Wuxi for interrogation. It is now learned that yesterday, Deputy Officer Wang interrogated the bandits again. The two bandits, Zhang Lou and Zhang Er, have confessed that they and six others planned to take the train to Longtan to rob a certain family. The other three took the opportunity to escape when the shooting occurred. Liang Zhaoxian was the instigator of this matter. According to the confession of Deputy Officer Wang, the bandit was ordered to be returned to custody. The acting regimental commander believes that this case is related to the security of the railway line and the circumstances are serious. Therefore, a special document was prepared, together with the three captured bandits, and it was decided to send personnel to the Nanjing Garrison Headquarters today (27th) for interrogation.

Ding Shuangsheng's Debt Disputes Still Difficult to Resolve 143

After the closure of Ding Shuangsheng Silk Shop in Dashiqiao, the county Chamber of Commerce was cleaning up the debt disputes. The creditors, Zhou Fenghao, Wang Zicheng, etc., filed a lawsuit with the county court to place a pre-trial seizure on a portion of the shop's inventory, believing that it was an obstacle to the principle of equality agreed upon by all creditors in the Chamber of Commerce the other day. Yesterday, they still convened a meeting at the Chamber of Commerce. The opinions of the creditors were divergent and there was no consensus. The chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, Qian Sunqing, announced on the spot that since a portion of the creditors had objections, the liquidation should be suspended from today and each creditor should proceed separately.

Two Chiefs of Departments Arrived in Wuxi One After Another 144

Sun Hongzhe (Kui Bo), Director of the Department of Construction of Jiangsu Province, and Deng Zaichen, Director of the Electricity Management Office, arrived in Wuxi by train from Zhenjiang at 2:00 p.m. the day before yesterday. Yesterday (26th), they went to the Wuxi-Yixing Road to inspect the project in order to send Tianjin workers to Wuxi to work. Niu Yongjian, Minister of Personnel Affairs, also arrived in Wuxi by special express train from Beijing at 9:00 p.m. the day before yesterday. He was accompanied by the Secretary-General, two secretaries, and Chen Youzhang, Chief of the Second Section, and twelve others. Yesterday morning, Zhu Jing'an, manager of the Minfeng Model Silk Factory, invited them to visit the factory. In the afternoon, Mr. Zhu hired a painted boat with a motor boat to accompany Minister Niu to visit scenic spots such as Meiyuan, Yuantouzhu, and Wanqingtang.

Changshu

Three Robberies in One Day 145

Zhou Zengfu, a rent collector (specializing in collecting rent and seeds for others) from Zhijiacun, Xintangkou, near Da Maojiaqiao outside the Shuibei Gate, is 72 years old and has two sons and a grandson. His family has a considerable amount of savings, which has been coveted by bandits. At about 5:00 a.m. on the 24th, five or six bandits came to the Zhou family and knocked on the door. Zengfu's grandson got up to open the door. As soon as the door was opened, many bandits rushed in and shouted for help. Zengfu heard the sound and fled outside. His grandson also ran out and shouted to catch the thief. The neighbors were awakened and came to catch the bandits. The bandits, fearing encirclement, howled and fled with the stolen goods. After checking, it was found that cash, foreign clothes, etc., worth about 200 yuan were robbed. In addition, there were many sailing ships traveling between this county and Luyuan. At about 3:00 a.m. on the 24th, a sailing ship was passing the Hujiao area outside the Ximen Gate when it suddenly encountered two bandit ships. The bandits were armed and blocked the sailing ship's way. They swarmed onto the ship, and the crew resisted and were beaten. Then they searched each passenger, and no one was spared. The loss was estimated at 800 to 900 yuan. At that time, a sailing ship from Xinzhuang Port was also sailing from the countryside and passed by here. It was also ordered to dock and the bandits divided up the ship and searched it thoroughly. As a result, cash and clothing bags worth about 1,000 yuan were lost. In addition, on the 13th, a Wang family passenger ship arrived at Wang Niqiao, Xinqiaobin River, Yuanhe District, and stayed there overnight. Unexpectedly, at midnight, a boat carrying several bandits robbed the Wang ship, resulting in a loss of more than 200 yuan and one crew member being stabbed.

Yangzhou

Robbery Case in Tangjiazhuang 146

The home of Tang Xuezheng, a resident of Tangjiazhuang near the Longwang Temple in the northern township of this county, was robbed the night before last by seven or eight bandits with pistols and box guns. The loss of clothing, foreign goods, and ornaments was estimated to be worth more than 400 yuan. Before leaving, they kidnapped his granddaughter-in-law and left a note limiting her to prepare a price of 7,000 yuan before the tenth day of the third lunar month to be picked up at Donghetou, Gaoyou. If overdue, the ticket will be torn. Tang rushed to the Public Security Bureau yesterday (24th) to request that a team be sent to rescue her.

In the Education Association, Chen Sibai, Qin Liankui, Qiao Yifan, Qi Xiyong, Qin Fengxiang, and Ma Yinbing had more votes.

Yu Jue Accuses Zhang Xiaoruo of Pursuing Property 148

Yu Jue from Suzhou sued Zhang Xiaoruo in the Nantong County Court to recover the property left by his wife Yu Shenshou before her death in Tong, which was valued at more than 100,000 yuan. The Civil Court opened the trial on the 25th. Zhang Xiaoruo hired a lawyer to file a petition for a one-week extension, which was immediately approved.

Court Investigates the Daho Round Body Abandonment Case 149

The branch court of the Shanghai-Yangtze River Dada Steamboat Company's Daho Round body abandonment case at Tianshenggang, all circles advocated strict investigation. The court prosecutor's office had once investigated and decided to continue the interrogation on the 27th, summoning the ship's Yi Yingfu, the crew member Wu Rangzhi, the director of the port's public security bureau Tang Ruiquan, and the journalist witness Zhong Zhenzhi and others, fourteen people in total.

Township Clearing Bureau Expedites Closing 150

The deadline for Nantong to hold the township clearing has expired and is now being rushed to a close in accordance with the provincial order and will be revoked at the end of this month.

Funing

Rampant Pirates at Miaowankou 151

Miaowan Seaport in this county is a thoroughfare for sea vessels entering and exiting. Now, it is being turned over to the sea vessels and they are exporting and fishing in succession. It is heard that the pirate Shen Guanlu and others are leading their wings and entrenched there, extremely rampant. Any ship that passes must pay an export fee of 20 to 100 yuan and must obtain a flag to hang on the mast before it can export. The pirates also have several sea vessels constantly patrolling the sea to avoid missing anyone. It is now heard that the ships that arrived earlier have been extorted because they could not resist. Now, more than 1,000 sea vessels in this county dare not export. If troops are not sent to suppress them in the shortest time, it is feared that the future of the fishing industry will be greatly affected.

Transfer of the Chief of the Public Security Sub-Bureau 152

Song Zhenbin, the chief of the Fourth Public Security Sub-Bureau of Yilin in this county, resigned from his position due to illness the other day, which has been approved. Now, the County Public Security Bureau has ordered Zhu Chunqi, the chief of the Second Public Security Sub-Bureau of Dongkan, to take over and has separately appointed Chen Yuetai, who once served as the chief of the General Affairs Section of the County Public Security Bureau, as the chief of the Second Public Security Sub-Bureau of Dongkan. It is heard that the two chiefs, Zhu and Chen, have already gone to take over their respective positions.

Pinghu

Minsheng Factory Closes and is Auctioned 153

The Provincial Minsheng Cotton Weaving Factory is located in this county and was previously run by Zhu Yushu. It was then ordered by the province to stop and close down. All of the factory's machinery and property were handed over to the county government for safekeeping. Now, it has been ordered by the Department of Construction to auction off the property. The machinery is calculated at 60% of the price and the property is calculated at 40% of the price. The minimum price is 1,640 yuan. Now, the county government has set May 1st at 9:00 a.m. for bids to be submitted and 2:00 p.m. that afternoon for the bids to be opened.

County Magistrate Strictly Prohibits Plowing and Planting on the Seawall Foot 154

The county government has received an order from the Department of Construction to investigate the Pinghu Seawall shore and found that the soil attached to the seawall is often eroded by the tides, endangering the seawall. It has been found that the villagers often plow and plant on the seawall foot. If this is allowed to accumulate over time, the seawall will be damaged beyond repair. The government should carefully investigate and handle the matter and report it. After receiving the order, the county government has ordered the Public Security Bureau to strictly prohibit it at any time.

Hangzhou

Opening of the Second National Exhibition 155

The opening ceremony of the Second National Goods Mobile Exhibition in Hangzhou City was held at 1:00 p.m. yesterday. About 500 representatives from Party and government agencies and guests from all walks of life attended. The Security Office also sent a military band to participate. Mayor Chen was busy with the national election and did not attend. Wu, the chief of the Social Affairs Section, presided over the meeting and delivered the opening speech. Jiang Senyu reported on the preparation process. Wu Zhongguo, the representative of the Department of Construction, and Qian Muming, the representative of the Exhibition Hall, all gave speeches. Finally, Wang Wenbin delivered a thank-you speech and led the visit to the exhibition hall and temporary commercial center for a week, which was very grand for a while.

Sports

The First Shanghai Municipal Secondary School Joint Sports Meet Concluded 157

Yesterday was sunny and hot... tens of thousands of spectators... fierce competition

Six Championship Winners

Group Men's A Jinan 丨 Men's B Nanyang 丨 丨 Women's Dongya

Individual Men's A Xie Quanxiang Chen Xingpei 丨 Men's B Deng Yingyuan 丨 Women Zhang Pingxian

Women's Long Jump and High Jump Results 丨 Two New National Records 158

The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education gathered more than 500 male and female athletes from 30 schools to hold the Shanghai Secondary School Joint Sports Meet. After three days of fierce competition, experiencing the changes of cold and hot days, once the championship positions were set and the front and rear rankings were divided, the first secondary school joint meeting was held

The Combined Association concluded successfully

Crowds Gathered 159

Yesterday, the sun shone brightly and the weather turned hot, as if it were early summer. All the events were finals and crowds gathered, numbering in the tens of thousands, which can be said to be the first record since the Far Eastern Games. The sound of applause and cheers rose from time to time, and the interest of the audience was no less than that of the participating athletes.

Fierce Competition 160

Yesterday, a total of fourteen finals were held, so the competition among the schools was extremely fierce. Even if there was no hope of winning a championship, they all tried their best to compete for fame. The group Men's A was like Jinan and Pudong, Men's B was like Nanyang and Pudong, and Women's was like Dongya and Southeast. Those who worked hard and hoped to create new records also tried their best, so the results were very good. It is hoped that all male and female athletes will work hard to the end.

National Record 161

(1) Women's Long Jump 丨 Four Meters 30 丨 Dongya Zhang Pingxian 丨

(2) Women's High Jump 丨 One Meter 26 丨 Southeast Zhang Binjin 丨

The competition created two new national records. (1) In the women's long jump on the first day, Zhang Pingxian of Dongya broke Wu Zongwu of Beiping's record of four meters 04 and Wu Meixian of the National Games' record of four meters with a score of four meters 30. The second place Qian Xingxu's score of four meters 21 also broke the national record. (2) On the third day, in the women's high jump, Zhang Baojin of Southeast broke Feng Falan of the National Games' record of one meter 22 and Sun Guiyun's record of one meter 25 in the Northeast Four Provinces Joint Games last year with a score of one meter 26. However, Xu Bangai of Nankai had a record of one meter 27 in the Tianjin City Games. Yesterday, the second place Yang Zhiren of Southeast's score of one meter 25 was also a new record.

Notes 176

Zhang Pingxian sets national record with 7.3 seconds in women's 50m preliminary.

Rare achievements are nothing more than the result of diligent training. At last year's Far Eastern Games, our country suffered many defeats. However, as the saying goes, "Don't be angry, just remember." As long as we practice patiently and persistently, there is no reason why we cannot avenge ourselves. Although the athletic performance at this city-wide middle school joint sports meet seems to be better than before, it is still hoped that everyone will continue to work harder and practice tirelessly, striving to win championships in international sports arenas. Because sports are not just a matter of one city or one country, but also of international importance. From a small perspective, it is indeed related to the development of physical education and the health of individuals, and thus to individual hygiene and longevity. However, extending this further, it is also closely related to the strength of the nation and its position and honor in the international arena. Today, I come to distribute prizes, and my heart is filled with an indescribable joy and delight. Now, I would like to congratulate all the winners on their victories. However, to those who did not win prizes, I sincerely hope that they will not be discouraged. Didn't I say earlier, "Don't be angry, just remember." Moreover, there is no certainty in victory and defeat. Victory and defeat are commonplace in military affairs. The prizes themselves are inanimate objects and cannot favor certain individuals. Each time, they will always end up in the hands of a few specific people. All those who did not win prizes this time should continue to work hard and practice every day without interruption. If they can do this, I am confident that they will be able to turn defeat into victory and win prizes in the next sports meet. The ancients said, "An iron ruler can be ground into an embroidery needle." Just imagine, if an iron ruler, which is so thick and large, can be ground into a small embroidery needle, how much easier are things like sports? As long as you put in some effort, there is no way you will not succeed. The so-called "Where there is a will, there is a way" is exactly what this victory is about. Those who have won prizes should not become complacent. They must continue to work hard and practice, just like those who have failed this time, and even more so. Only then can they maintain their past glory, retain the prizes they have won, and have hope of winning prizes in the future. Otherwise, like a firecracker, it will make a loud noise and then be gone. Why would one be satisfied with that? These are a few words I want to say to everyone before distributing the prizes. Now, I will begin giving out the prizes according to the list.

The results of all events in this competition are quite remarkable, and the breaking of national records in women's high jump and long jump is especially noteworthy. All prizes for the top three in total scores for groups and individuals will be awarded today, and the rest can be collected from the Education Bureau tomorrow by the respective schools.

Notice of New Rules 186

Many were disqualified at this meeting for violating the latest track and field regulations due to ignorance, so we are specifically listing them to inform all schools. (1) New rule for track races: Disqualification after two false starts. Many were penalized in the preliminaries for this reason. (2) New rule for hurdles: Touching or knocking down a hurdle is strictly prohibited and will result in disqualification. Even touching a hurdle causing it to wobble will result in disqualification. (3) New rule: No ties for places. If scores are the same, a final will be held until a winner is determined. Therefore, there were no ties for places at this track and field meet due to this rule.

Free Talk

World Anecdotes 190

— Haike

Berliners have recently been infected with the American habit of making phone calls. The city has a total of 472,000 telephones, and there are 1.3 million calls made every day.

Although the treatment of university professors in England and the United States is better than that of educators in the East, and those with special knowledge are world-renowned, their salaries are still inferior to other professions. Very few of them can earn 1,500 pounds a year.

The British Museum in London has an average of 800 people reading in the reading room every day.

According to a survey by British sociologists, the total number of slaves in the world who have lost their personal freedom is no less than four million.

The number of divorced men and women in the United States is exactly offset by the number of newly married men and women. For example, if ten people get married, ten people get divorced. Overall, the number of marriages is decreasing day by day, while the number of divorces is increasing day by day.

British gold leaf craftsmen have the best skills in the world. They can beat a piece of gold foil one and a quarter inches square and one thousandth of an inch thick into sixteen gold leaves, each five inches square.

Extensive Use of Spring Flowers 191

— Yang Yixiao

Spring flowers have the widest range of uses. Lilac can be used for powder, peony can be used in medicine, camellia can be used for hairdressing, crabapple can be used to make honey, redbud can be used as a bed, peony can be used to cover houses, rose can be used to make water, daphne can be used for tea, sweet-scented osmanthus can be used to brew wine, poppy can be used to cook porridge, cymbidium can be used to induce childbirth, wisteria can be used to make incense boxes, mimosa can be used as a pillow, Chinese flowering crabapple can be used to make bait, and hibiscus can be used for hair ornaments. The various spring flowers bloom at different times, so their uses are also different.

Anecdotes After the Daji Disaster 192

— Yu

The Daji steamship of the Dada Shipping Company was burned in Longjusha, Jiangbei, with countless crew and passenger deaths. According to the latest investigation, the Zhang Huanggang Public Security Bureau recovered 398 corpses, the Xinshenggang recovered 11 corpses, and the Xingang recovered another 5 corpses. More than 210 people were rescued and returned to Shanghai by specially dispatched ships and fishing boats. Another 7 people died from the cold after being rescued, so the total death toll reached more than 411, which is a major disaster. It is said that among these victims, there were some who made a fortune because of it. A certain person, with great courage, when the fire broke out on the ship, the passengers were only concerned with their lives, and money was nothing more than an external thing, thinking that it was a burden, so they untied everything they had on their bodies, leaving only their shirts and pants, and then jumped into the water, fearing that heavy clothes and too much money would prevent them from floating on the water to wait for rescue. This person relied on his good swimming skills to take the foreign bills of everyone and put them in his arms, swam away, and survived, thus making a fortune. Also, at that time, the passengers not only untied everything they had on their bodies, but also threw their boxes and cages into the water in groups, and people clung to them to avoid sinking. Who would have thought that the fishermen were cruel and took the objects with bamboo poles without saving people. Those who clung to the objects and tried to float were pushed into the water, causing many deaths, which was no different from being killed by the fishermen. Afterwards, three fishermen were arrested and shot, which everyone applauded. There was also a strange incident. A passenger named Mou Yi hid 2,400 yuan in banknotes. After entering the water, he floated up and down near a fishing boat. He asked the fishing boat for help, saying that he had money. The fisherman immediately helped him onto the boat and asked how much he had. Mou Yi truthfully told him and offered to split it evenly. The fisherman ordered him to take it out and count it. There was no mistake. He was not satisfied with splitting it evenly and wanted to swallow it all. He carried Mou Yi into the sea and pushed him into the water when he was not paying attention, and then he died. The next day at midnight, his son suddenly dreamed that Mou Yi told him about the murder and told his son to avenge him. He could visit a fisherman surnamed Wang, and the banknotes were still on the boat and would not deny it. His son woke up in shock and went to the scene of the accident as he said. He asked about the Wang surname fishing boat, and everyone said that there was one that had not been seen for a day and did not know where it had gone. While he was asking and answering, everyone suddenly pointed to a boat and said, "Here it is! Here it is! It's that boat!" His son hurriedly boarded the boat and dragged the person on the boat to the government, accusing him of his father's dream. The person on the boat did not admit it, so he searched his boat and found 2,400 yuan in banknotes, so he was able to confirm it. The official continued to interrogate him, and he finally confessed to the matter. In this era of scientific enlightenment, whether there are ghosts or not is still a matter of debate among spiritualists. This is indeed an excellent research material.

Special Report 193

From May 1st, this publication will launch a "Novella Rotary Club", with famous writers Tianxu Wosheng, Wang Dun'gen, Bao Tianxiao, Jiang Hongjiao, Xu Zhuodai, Yao Suifeng, Zhang Henshui, Cheng Xiaoqing, and Cheng Zhanlu taking turns to write various short novellas, each about 10,000 words, all with rich emotions and beautiful writing. Readers, please pay attention.

A Trip to Dongting Lake 194

— Rui Hongchu

In this spring day, with the gentle breeze, reading the old saying "Don't let the good spring days pass, the hardest thing is the wind and rain of old friends", the desire to travel arises. Therefore, I invited Jin Binglan, Jin Meisheng, Chen Junbei, Qian Fusheng, and others to travel to Dongting Lake. On the 9th of the month, we arrived at Suzhou by early train and stayed at the Dongwu Hotel. The next day, we took the Baoxing boat to Hengxi and landed to visit the Hengxi School. The principal, Mr. Jin Bofu, warmly welcomed us. The school was well-organized, with a library equipped with various magazines and novels for students to browse after class. There was also a public reading room with Shenbao, Xinwenbao, Wuxian Daily, Mingbao, and City-Township Public Gazette for people to read. Hengxi's municipal administration has been greatly renovated compared to last year, and commerce is developed and the population is dense. In the afternoon, we changed to a gasoline boat to Lianxi Town to visit Cai Lian Tang. It is said that during the Warring States period, King Wu favored Xi Shi, and this was where lotus flowers were picked in those years. There is Cai Lian Bridge, and the traces of King Wu seem to be still faintly discernible. That night, we stayed at Jinjiafang. At dawn, we hired a folk boat and went straight to Dongting. After six hours, we arrived at Longtou Mountain, which has a large stone cave called Long Cave. It is more than ten feet wide and about five feet high. The cave is dark, and you can only enter with the help of candlelight. Cowards dare not enter. According to the mountain people, there are three entrances to this cave, and there are stone benches, stone tables, and stone beds. Outside the cave, a stone tablet is inscribed with "Ninth Cave in the World" by Mr. Yu Quyuan. We then went to Piaomiao Peak. The mountain road is winding and rugged, and it is not easy to walk. After two hours, we reached the top of the mountain. Looking out, the Taihu Lake is the same color as the sky, and the waves undulate like ten thousand horses galloping. It is indeed a spectacle. After walking dozens of steps, we arrived at Shigon Mountain, which has a Guiyun Cave. A statue of Guanshiyin is enshrined in the cave, next to a couplet saying "Clouds stack thousands of layers at the mouth of Guiyun Cave, the moon circles over Mingyue Bay". To the east is Cuiyun Xuan, a small building with a corner and a secluded scenery, built by Mr. Feng Xingcun, a famous scholar of the Ming Dynasty. Above it is Laihe Pavilion, with cliffs on both sides. We climbed up the stone steps, facing south from the mountain, to Sunset Cave. There is an inverted tower in the cave, which is extremely dangerous. Above Sunset Cave is a line of sky, more than ten feet deep. We ventured forward and reached its peak. It was getting late, so we hurriedly took the original boat back to Lianxi, which was already lit with thousands of lights. The next day, we returned to Shanghai and wrote this down to leave a footprint.

Anecdotes from the Art World 195

— Ke Ding'an

Mr. Su Kan, the master of Hai Cang Tower, never casually commented on the calligraphy and paintings of his contemporaries. However, he highly praised the flowers and birds painted by Ma Mengrong, saying, "The essence of realistic painting lies in distinguishing between elegance and vulgarity. Works filled with intention are often elegant, while those brimming with vigor tend to be vulgar. Modern people love to imitate He Shaoji and Cang Shuo, whose forceful style I often find questionable. When I look at the works of Wu Rangzhi and Li Futang, they are exceptionally refined and extraordinary. Mr. Mengrong is a close acquaintance of Rangzhi and Futang, as discerning individuals recognize." He also inscribed the two characters "Rong Zhai" as a gift to him. Mr. Zeng Nongran once said, "Among contemporary flower and bird painters, Mengrong should be praised for his elegant brushwork, demonstrating his specialized learning." Both Zheng and Zeng were senior figures in the art world, and their praise for Mengrong speaks volumes about the divine quality of his works. Mr. Cai Yuanpei once remarked, "The difference between the literati and the academy styles in our country lies in the fact that the works of literati are mostly lively in spirit and convey profound meaning, but excessive freedom can lead to looseness. The works of the academy are mostly precise in their ruled-line paintings and meticulously realistic in their depictions, but excessive restraint can lead to rigidity. Mr. Mengrong strikes a balance between the two styles, adopting the strengths of both, resulting in outstanding and artistically valuable works." Li Shu'an, a respected elder in calligraphy and painting, said, "Mengrong's paintings draw inspiration from nature and integrate the past and present. He paints what others cannot and dares not paint, creating meticulous compositions with effortless brushstrokes, each stroke unique and transformed, sweeping away commonplace forms, truly a masterpiece for the ages, worthy of admiration."... Other famous artists such as Wu Changshuo and Wang Yiting also presented inscriptions to Mengrong, who kept them hidden in his chest, unwilling to let the world know. Yesterday, I visited him and, after rummaging through his collection, I extracted a few selections to share with those who appreciate Mengrong's paintings.

Wang Dongpei, a renowned figure from Nanjing, is famed for his poetry, calligraphy, and painting throughout the north and south of the Yangtze River. He and Mengrong have long been spiritual companions. They plan to arrange a joint exhibition of their works in the spring and summer for connoisseurs to appreciate. Major publishing houses in Shanghai are eagerly seeking Mengrong's works for widespread circulation. It is said that hundreds of people aspire to learn from him. All of this demonstrates that only someone with genuine artistry could deserve such honor, hence this record to express my admiration.

A New Short Biography of Zhou Zidexin 196

— Tianxu Wosheng

Zhou Zidexin is the beloved son of my friend, Mr. Shanjiang. He was born with innate intelligence and showed extraordinary qualities even in infancy. His mother taught him characters, which he recognized as if he had known them before. At the age of three, he could read books, reciting anything he heard without fail. By the age of seven, he understood literature and reason. His father taught him history books and English arithmetic, which he remembered after a single glance, as clearly as if they were on the palm of his hand. He practiced calligraphy, focusing on Yan Zhenqing's style, striving to capture its essence. Therefore, the people of his hometown all regarded him as a child prodigy. In August of the Gengwu year, he suddenly felt ill and knew that his time was short. He asked for paper and brush on his pillow and drafted a will of one hundred and twenty characters to bid farewell to his parents. I was fortunate to see a printed copy of it. The handwriting was vigorous, and the spirit was extraordinary, resembling Yan Zhenqing's "Draft of a Requiem to My Nephew." It is truly rare for a fifteen-year-old child to be so intelligent. Mr. and Mrs. Shanjiang had only this one son, and their hopes were high, but he was suddenly taken away by Heaven, causing them unbearable grief and a desire to die. There was no elixir to prolong his life, nor any technique to restore his soul. So, a hundred days later, they came to me and said that they had seen this child in a dream, claiming that his past life was as a high-ranking monk, yet his words and actions were just as ordinary as usual, saying that if he had the chance, he would be reborn into their family. His mother's infatuation with this idea deepened, and she even inscribed a mark on his palm as he was dying, perhaps out of the sincerity of her spirit, hoping that his soul could be autonomous. At first, I could only sigh and offer condolences, unable to find words of comfort. I thought that human life in this world is like a dream. If one has a sweet dream, one still has lingering fondness after waking. Therefore, I regret that his dream ended too soon. If it were a nightmare, causing unspeakable suffering in spirit, then one would struggle with all one's might to wake up and would surely rejoice and never wish to relive the previous dream. That can be said with certainty. My friend's love for his son of fifteen years was met with the pain of losing sight in an instant, like a half-cooked millet dream being abruptly awakened, making one feel that the dream was sweet and blissful, and therefore all the more regrettable. However, no matter what, the dream must eventually end. As for the length of the dream and the earliness or lateness of waking, they are mostly created by the mind and are within one's own control. Everyone who has a son believes that he is the hope of the family line, but in reality, this is just a policy to make fools of the people, making them create farmers for the country. However, in today's world, with the well-field system long abandoned and nations competing for survival, everyone uses the weak to feed the strong. If we do not compete with the world, we must haggle over our own selfish desires, hoping for filial sons and virtuous grandsons to protect our inheritance, and hoping to enjoy their sacrifices after we die. I truly feel that this is incredibly foolish, so it is no wonder that nightmares are so frequent. Who in life does not die? To die at a time when it is impossible to promise anything is to be complete. To die while still having parents but no wife and children is especially fortunate. We drift through half our lives, watching the rivers and mountains decline day by day without being able to save them, only feeling that the suffering we endure is getting worse and worse, regretting that we are dying so late. Compared to Zhou Zidexin, I can only praise him without reservation. What is the use of mourning? It is only that my friend and his wife are still searching for a dream within a dream. If their dream truly comes true and human life lasts only a thousand years, my friend and his wife will see their son's sons and grandsons live and die. I do not know how they will be able to resolve the sorrow, joy, suffering, and pain they will experience in their own minds and bodies. Therefore, I sigh and offer condolences with the deepest emotion, unable to find words of comfort. As for his words and deeds, they are detailed in my friend's own "Record of Grief," so I will not repeat them here. I believe that what is worth passing on is not his early learning and intelligence, but his ability to maintain a clear mind at the time of his death, still able to write from his pillow as calmly as usual. His filial piety is commendable, and his willpower is extraordinary. As the saying goes, "Knowing when to stop allows one to be at peace," something that ordinary people cannot do, let alone at the time of death. As for the theory that his past life was as a high-ranking monk, if it is not just the ravings of a dream, then his spirit is immortal and must be able to be autonomous and free. However, I believe that his desire for rebirth is still clinging to a lower form.

Travels in India (36) 197

— Linghua

Success in business is not easily achieved. In 1756, the Indians retook Calcutta. Three years later, in 1759, the British, under Clive, recaptured it and signed a treaty with the Muslim leaders to subdue them. The construction of the artillery fort was completed in 1753. These events all took place in the 17th century. Over a hundred years of gradual management followed until Queen Victoria promulgated a decree on November 1, 1858, declaring India under British rule. Thus, the British completed their great work in governing India (72 years ago to this day).

Investigation is not easy; people are accustomed to not noticing. For example, if you ask someone who has lived in Shanghai and Nanjing for a long time about the population of Nanjing, they will likely be unable to answer. I repeatedly asked Indian friends about the population of Calcutta, and some said over five million. I did not believe it and consulted books to find a clearer answer: just over 1,327,000 people. Bombay, on the other hand, has only 728,000 people. This place's commerce rivals that of Bombay and Madras, hence the name "London of the East." India has three major ports: Bombay, Madras, and Calcutta.

This place has two seasons a year. From November to February is winter, from March to June is summer, and from July to October is the wet season with much rain. The most rainfall is in August, the hottest month is May, and the coldest month is late December, but only a light jacket is needed to get by. The nights are quite cold, so cotton clothing is advisable.

On the 22nd, I visited the Kali Temple, also known as the old master of Calcutta. It is located south of Calcutta, as indicated by the large characters "Kali Ghat" on trams and other vehicles. The temple is a few minutes' walk from the stop. It is not very large but new, consisting of only a main hall, which is also not grand, and a lobby outside. Before entering the temple, many men asked for money, which I found unpleasant because it was overwhelming. If I gave to one, they would surround me. The temple was crowded with men and women, shoulder to shoulder like the City God Temple in Shanghai, but I found the jostling of dark-skinned, bare-chested Indians unbearable, so I did not want to push my way in and only lingered outside the window. Many birds were perched above, leaving droppings below, making it impossible to stay. My companion had already been hit by bird droppings on the head, and my hat was also stained. The gatekeeper charged two annas to open the door, allowing a glimpse into the black abyss, but it was impossible to see what was inside. Indian friends held incense, bowed, and entered, offering flowers or having flower garlands placed on their heads and necks, but they had to pay for it. I walked dozens of steps west of the temple and saw many vendors selling various incarnations of Kali. Their stories are difficult to trace. Indian scholars say that they are transformed from the same god as Krishna, one male and one female. Not far to the west is a small river with muddy water about two or three feet deep. In the morning, it was still cool, and dozens of men and women were bathing in the river at the same time. I asked why, and they said that this was not bathing but being baptized, immersing themselves completely in the water. I then realized the story of the Jordan River in Christianity and the practice of immersion, where one must immerse the entire body to show reverence. This river is a branch of the old Ganges River, a small but world-famous holy river. There were water taps on the riverbank. I thought that it would be fine to use clean spring water from the taps for baptism, so why enter the muddy waters? There was an ancient temple on the riverbank with various transformations and strange shapes painted on the walls, as well as various idols, half-intact and half-broken, resembling humans and ghosts. I could not help but sigh at the fact that animals have become humans and that their sins are the same as the river, constantly flowing and not knowing when they will be cleansed.

Business News

Gold Speculation Rises Thirty-Four Taels Last Week 198

Major players covering short positions, bulls adding to their positions

Daily fluctuations exceed ten taels

Since Monday (April 22nd), the big silver bar rose to 1875, and the silver price rose to 375, so the opening price of the June gold contract was 699 taels, a decrease of 7.5 taels compared to last Saturday. Soon after, speculators pushed the price up by 6.7 taels to 706.7 taels, almost reaching the limit. Internal factors were also favorable. In the afternoon, the situation suddenly reversed, with foreign banks showing signs of contraction while domestic banks expanded. Many in the market were selling, so the quoted price was reduced by half a level. Dadetai and Hengxing covered short positions for a total of more than 4,000 contracts, and other firms followed suit, buying heavily and causing the price to rise sharply to 720 taels. The closing price was 17.8 taels, an increase of 11.3 taels. After the market closed, the price rose a total of 21 taels. Looking back at the next day, the big silver bar fell slightly to 1875, and the silver price fell slightly to 375. The quoted price also shrank by half a level. The domestic market followed closely. The market first sold and then bought, and the gold market opened high at 718.5 taels. Dalien and Guangbang sold and retreated to 15.5 taels, then Xinxing and Hengyuan covered short positions, pushing the price up to 27.5 taels. In the afternoon, sellers saw strength and the closing price was 20 taels, still an increase of 2.2 taels. The entire day also saw a fluctuation of 12 taels. On Wednesday, the big silver bar fell slightly by 0.0625, and the silver market decreased by 0.125. The quoted price remained unchanged, then changed to shrink by half a level. The internal market showed strength, and Chinese merchants rushed to buy. The gold market initially opened slightly lower by 1.5 taels at 718.5 taels, which was indeed due to the slight shrinkage of the big silver bar and a lack of confidence. Later, rumors spread that a certain bank planned to transport cash out of the country, and major players covered short positions, pushing the price up by more than 30 taels. There were also rumors from the United States that British banks would close, fearing that exchange rates would tighten sharply and causing the price to rise to 35 taels. In the afternoon, Qianchangxiang bought on behalf of a Shanghai client, reaching as high as 40 taels, and the closing price was 39.1 taels, a further increase of 19.1 taels. The continuous rise for three days totaled 32.6 taels. The total daily fluctuation was 21.5 taels. The next day, the big silver bar shrank again by 0.25, and the silver market shrank by 0.375. The quoted price also shrank by one level. The domestic market was firm but weak, clearly showing strength on the surface but weakness underneath. Banks were still willing to sell, but the situation was the opposite of the previous day. The market rushed to close positions. The gold market initially opened down 4.1 taels at 34 taels. This was due to the poor performance of the big silver bar and the influence of American buying. Later, there was more buying, reaching 39.5 taels. Then Guangbang and others sold, causing the price to fall. In the afternoon, the price suddenly broke through 30 taels and closed at 28.3 taels, a reversal after many days of continuous rise. The drop was 10.08 taels, with a fluctuation of 14 taels. The next day, the big silver bar rebounded by 0.3125, and the silver price increased by half a cent. The quoted price also increased by one level. The domestic market was flat, and those who were trapped continued to buy. The gold market opened slightly lower by 1.8 taels at 26.5 taels. Buyers were active, pushing the price to 27 taels, then back to 24.1 taels. In the afternoon, certain banks bought, causing the price to rise to 39 taels. Due to eager sellers, the price retreated to 33 taels, and the closing price was 35.5 taels, a rebound of 7.2 taels. The total daily fluctuation was 14.9 taels. On Saturday, the big silver bar shrank by 0.0625, the silver price decreased by 0.375, and the quoted price shrank by half a level. The domestic market was stable, and the gold market opened up 7 taels at 740.5 taels. Later, the price rose from 40.02 taels to 46 taels, with fluctuations of two or three taels, but there were no special changes. At noon, the price suddenly broke through the 40-tael mark, closing at 39.5 taels within the mark. The closing price was 40.08 taels, an increase of 5.3 taels compared to the previous day. The difference in the half-day was 6.5 taels. The margin for spot gold was about 12 to 11 taels higher. The high and low prices of British, American, Indian silver markets and exchange rates are listed below.

Category Highest Price Lowest Price Change from Previous Saturday

Recent Big Silver Bar 13 pence 5 13 pence 875 Shrunk 0.0625

Distant Big Silver Bar 13 pence 4375 12 pence 375 Shrunk 0.0625

Bond Prices Trended Lower Last Week 201

Total Weekly Turnover Exceeded 43 Million Yuan
