Wednesday reached 9.3 million, and Monday and Friday were both over 8 million. Wednesday and the weekend each had over 6 million. The spot market was very sluggish, with only 62,800 yuan, of which Yili Customs accounted for 30,000 yuan, and the rest were only several thousand yuan. As for the changes in bond prices, the bond market environment was as depressed as before. Major players did not make any large-scale entries or exits. With the settlement period approaching, the market was particularly cautious. Therefore, although the market continued to be quite active, the supply and demand situation remained balanced, and bond prices were more sluggish than the previous week. The only exception was Wednesday, when rumors of a price drop of 6 or 7 jiao spread, resulting in a larger fluctuation. The remaining days saw fluctuations of only a few jiao. Cotton Yarn Market Was Dispersed Last Week 202

The yarn market trend was extremely dispersed last week, with a risk of market price declining. Overseas cotton yarn conditions trended downwards, and sales of spot yarn were not very smooth. Consequently, market sentiment was extremely weak. Most small traders were cautious as the season was gradually entering a slack period. In addition, there was a large amount of inventory of 10-count coarse yarn, so sellers were bold and exerted more pressure. Although major buyers remained unmoved, the surrounding environment was unfavorable, and it was difficult to support the market alone. At the end of the week, the American cotton grade three slightly improved, and the market slightly rebounded. However, Ruidai liquidated a large number of long positions, and the market was compressed by this action, causing the table to suddenly loosen. It was observed that Shanbang and two yarn factories covered short positions. Judging from the overall trend of the yarn market, it is currently in a consolidation phase. The statistics of spot yarn purchased by each bank show that 7,785 bales were purchased. The most purchases were made by the inland and Guangdong areas, while other banks had average purchases. The marked yarn prices fell for one or two weeks, and slightly rose for four or five weeks. At the end of the week, most long positions were liquidated, resulting in a drop. As a result, the prices of each month were the same as last week for nearby months, and the distant months rose by two, three, or four qian. The total turnover for the whole week was 139,000 bales. The lowest price for grade three yarn was 123.5 yuan in the distant month, and the rebound resulted in a similar situation to last week. The amount of bales purchased by each bank is recorded below.

Grain and Rice Market Was Oscillating 205

Zhabei 206

Yesterday, the source of arrival was not much. Sales were affected by the sunny weather. The Northern polished rice stored in the river cannot be kept for long in warm weather. Therefore, although the initial opening of Northern polished rice was stable, it soon weakened. The price of top-quality polished rice opened at approximately 12.3 yuan. The inferior quality of the thin rice was mediocre. Only high-quality goods were slightly active. The overall market was slightly discounted. The customer demand for Yangshe indica rice and Shanghai indica rice was poor. The market was not active. The price was initially high but then softened. The value of Yin Yuan has dropped since it was raised. The sales market is sluggish and the situation is weak. The value of Special Yin Yuan opened at around 10.5 yuan.

South Shanghai 207

Yesterday, more than ten boats arrived, and sales in the main street were initially brisk but then slowed down. The price of early-harvest polished white rice was initially high due to the remaining momentum from the Northern market, but it softened due to the sunny weather. However, the price only oscillated by half a jiao to one jiao. The thin rice and early rice from the South Bank were active in the morning but rare and sluggish in the afternoon. However, the best quality goods fluctuated. The sales of Yin Yuan were stagnant and the willingness to buy was quiet. There was no rise in the price of Yin Yuan and top-quality goods were already too high, so the market continued to decline. The market price was discounted by nearly a jiao.

Silk and Tea: Last Week's Silk Market Lacked Vitality 208

Last week, overseas silk weaving factories heavily relied on rayon for summer silk fabrics, coupled with slow sales of spring silk and weak inventories. Silk merchants adopted a passive attitude, leading to a significant decrease in raw silk consumption. Telegrams from Shanghai's Chinese silk businesses to Europe and America were not forwarded, resulting in a lifeless market atmosphere. Japanese and Italian silk inventories remained substantial, making it difficult to clear them before the new silk season. Fortunately, China experienced a poor silkworm cocoon harvest last year, resulting in limited silk inventory. Although a sell-out is expected, small silk merchants are suffering significant losses due to high purchase prices. Reports from Zhejiang indicate a poor spring silkworm season, with 70-80% of silkworm eggs abandoned due to cold weather and rain. Consequently, manufacturers are reluctant to release new cocoon silk. Only over 200 bales of silk were traded last week, with over 700 bales exported. Overseas Chinese silk prices were nominally stable but effectively weak due to exchange rate fluctuations. Qimen Bai Hao Tea Begins Harvesting and Production 209

Qimen County's new tea crop is benefiting from favorable weather this year. Tea bushes in the tea gardens began to bud after Qingming Festival. Recent warm and rainy weather has made it easier for tender shoots to emerge. Famous tea houses in Qizhuang that produce Bai Hao tribute tea have already started picking tender buds and processing them. If the warm weather continues without cold spells, formal garden opening for the first flush may occur within days. Various tea houses are currently planning to transport tea to foreign merchants, dispatching personnel to establish branches in various tea-producing areas to set up weighing scales for purchasing and to supervise tea farmers in harvesting and sun-drying tender leaves to avoid repeating last year's mistake of allowing leaves to become old and coarse, leading to rejection by foreign merchants.

Recent News from Hunan and Hubei Tea Regions 210

The provinces of Hunan and Hubei are important tea-producing regions in China, with vast producing areas and significant output. In prosperous years, red tea exports from Hunan and Hubei accounted for about half of the total red tea exports. However, in the past decade, frequent wars and banditry have led to a decline in the rural economy, and tea bushes are no longer cultivated as diligently as before. As a result, output has declined daily. Those engaged in the red and green tea business have also suffered from high costs, tight sales, and sluggish exports, resulting in unbearable losses. This year, the Hunan provincial authorities, in an effort to revitalize the tea industry, telegraphed the Shanghai Municipal Government to invite tea merchants to purchase tea in Hunan and to protect their safety. However, due to sluggish exports, many boxes of Hunan and Hubei tea remain in Shanghai warehouses uncleared. Therefore, tea merchants' interest in tea trade in Hunan and Hubei has waned, and it appears difficult to actively restore the former prosperity. Currently, tea firms in Hankou and tea merchants in the two provinces are hesitant about whether to promptly go to the mountains to manage tea affairs. However, the various types of green tea in North China stores are gradually seeing improved sales as transportation on the Pinghan Railway and other routes resumes. In the future, there may be a large volume of purchases of green tea, which may show some improvement compared to the past.

Limited Progress Expected in Qiupu Tea Market 211

Qiupu borders Qimen and Fuliang and is a famous tea-producing area in central Anhui. Its convenient transportation and fast shipping have led to an increasing number of foreign tea firms operating in the area. In the previous two years, excessive numbers of tea houses led to a sharp rise in mountain prices and doubled costs. Many ended up suffering losses. This year, existing tea houses, recognizing the tight credit situation and the lack of improvement in foreign sales, and considering that the quality of tea leaves here is not as good as that of Qimen, are mostly adopting a wait-and-see approach for the sake of caution. Their intention is that they will not act until mountain prices fall significantly and credit conditions ease. Currently, there are very few people preparing to open tea processing areas, which is not as lively as in previous years. It seems that the tea market will not see any progress for the time being.

A Sudden Surge in Fabric Sales Due to Hot Weather 212

Yesterday's sudden hot weather caused a surge in retail fabric sales. Items like serge, tweed, water tweed, satin, and drill were in high demand, mostly for making unlined summer clothing for men and women. Business was particularly brisk in the Qipan Street area of Henan Road. Prices were slightly lower than ten days ago, due to a drop in wholesale prices, which translated to cheaper retail prices. Tailors who make Western-style clothing also continued to purchase fabrics like flannel, Barathean cloth, and yellow twill.

Woolen Goods and Fabrics Experience Price Drops 213

Recently, the prices of woolen goods and fabrics have experienced widespread declines. Items like tribute cloth, serge, tweed, water tweed, pantou cloth, Barathean cloth, and raincoat fabric have all seen sharp price drops. Currently, single-sided "boiling water" American raincoat fabric has fallen to 5.15 taels. Rongtai, Deki, and Yongfeng's colored plaid water tweed and diagonally dotted drill, which were selling for 4.5-4.6 taels last week, have now fallen to 4.2-4.3 taels. Dongfang 3008 medium-thick serge is priced at 3.925 taels, and 3001 is priced at 3 taels. Old Sassoon, Tianjialuo's miscellaneous colors are selling for 2.65 taels, and Ningfeng's "Going to a Banquet" fabric is priced at 2.55 taels, a price decrease of 0.1-0.2 taels compared to the past. Yuanqing tribute cloth, regardless of quality, has dropped by an average of 0.05-0.1 taels per yard. Deki 2488 has been reduced to 4.9 taels, SSS to 2.1 taels, and Rongtai's old brand 15330 remains at 7.75 taels. Anli's "Five Old Friends Meeting" is priced at 6.5 taels.

Two Important Telegrams from the Municipal Federation

Telegram Congratulating Foreign Minister Wang 215

To Wang Chongjian, Minister of Foreign Affairs of the National Government in Nanjing. Reports have been received that the Sino-Dutch and Sino-Nicaraguan agreements on the abolition of consular jurisdiction were formally signed the day before yesterday, and that negotiations on the abolition of extraterritoriality with the United Kingdom and the United States are also close to completion. The news has spread, and the entire nation is delighted. You, Minister, have worked hard for the party and the country, and are a pillar in the legal field, reversing the collapsing tide and washing away the shame of our ancestors. Your political achievements are evident, and your reputation is greatly enhanced. Upon hearing this, we cannot contain our joy. However, the one million citizens in the Shanghai concessions have long been trapped under the power of imperialists. Even the analogy of being in deep water and scorching fire is insufficient to express their pain. Considering civil lawsuits with imperialists, countless cases have been suppressed and unresolved within a year. As for criminal lawsuits, there have been many wrongful convictions that have never been cleared up in Shanghai alone. If Shanghai is like this, how can the other concessions be an exception? Now that the Netherlands and Nicaragua know to respect each other's national systems and legal rights, our country should treat them as friendly nations. The United Kingdom and the United States, known for their civilization and progress, should not hesitate excessively in this spirit and understanding of mutual respect. In the midst of celebration, we respectfully offer a word of advice, requesting that you further invigorate your spirit and strive to complete the remaining tasks of abolishing extraterritoriality in the shortest possible time. With legal rights unified and national integrity complete, take another step and vigorously implement the work of abolishing unequal treaties to achieve the goal of freedom and equality and to comfort the spirit of the late Premier in heaven and to fulfill the earnest hope of the entire nation. Respectfully submitted. The Preparatory Committee of the Shanghai Special District Citizens' Federation salutes you.

Telegram Presented to Representatives of the National Assembly 216

To the Honorable Representatives of the National Assembly in Nanjing. The late patriots knew that the United Kingdom poisoned China with opium, and due to unfortunate military defeats in war, the Treaty of Nanjing was forced upon us in August 1842, a great shame. Tracing back the causes, it was due to the administration of the Manchu barbarians and the presence of treacherous officials in the court. From then on, the great powers regarded China as their prey, freely slaughtering and daring not to resist. From 1842 to the present, a total of ninety years, there have been fifteen instances of losing territory, fifteen instances of losing tributary states, and eight instances of losing territorial waters and straits. There have also been six instances of incomplete sovereignty over territorial waters. As for the loss of legal rights, the establishment of concessions, the agreement on tariffs, and the granting of indemnities, these cannot be fully described in a short space. Observing the great powers' military aggression, cultural aggression, economic aggression, and so on, their unreasonable and barbaric policies have all been directed at us, using every means to bind and oppress us, in an attempt to shatter China's national system and destroy the nation before stopping. Our late Premier awakened the people, promoted the Three Principles of the People, and devoted himself to the revolution and the construction of the Republic of China. Now that military administration has been unified and political tutelage is being implemented, our party comrades are all diligently following his will and striving to complete the remaining tasks. The National Assembly has been convened, unequal treaties should be abolished, and the responsibility to complete the revolution must be actively pursued. The one million five hundred thousand citizens in Shanghai who are located in the concessions created by unequal treaties feel the suffering and pain most deeply and acutely. In short, the Shanghai concessions are semi-colonies, the Shanghai concessions are breeding grounds for all evils, human rights are swept away, and there is no light of day. If these concessions are not recovered, then China's sovereignty will not be complete, and society will not be stable. It is truly essential to recover them as soon as possible to save our compatriots and complete our territory. We respectfully request that your assembly's representatives quickly resolve to abolish unequal treaties and recover the Shanghai concessions and all other concessions in the country, and invigorate your spirit to complete the revolution. It would be fortunate for the citizens of Shanghai and fortunate for the Chinese nation. The Preparatory Committee of the Shanghai Special District Citizens' Federation salutes you.

Temporary purchase of 50 mu of land

90 yuan per mu

Since the decision to establish the new Shanghai County seat in Beiqiao Town in the Third District, Wu Wenhua, Chairman of the Relocation Committee, has urged the Construction Bureau staff to actively proceed with the work without sparing effort. Sincerely, The Shanghai Coal Industry Association."

Declaration of the Establishment of the Shanghai Publishing Industry Workers' Union 221

Declaration of the Establishment of the Shanghai Publishing Industry Workers' Union (titles omitted): Our Union held its first representative assembly on February 28 of this year and was formally established in accordance with the law. Now, at the beginning of our organization, we dare to briefly describe the mission we bear and the path we will take for future endeavors:

Regarding Organizational Aspects 222

First, regarding the number of members, although there are no accurate statistics on the total number of workers in the publishing industry in the city, it must be at least around 20,000. However, at present, only the members of the Commercial Press Office, numbering less than 4,000, have gathered under the banner of our Union. The remaining 16,000 are enduring a haggard and groaning existence under the oppression of iron-fisted capitalists, which is truly heartbreaking. Our Union is determined to overcome all difficulties in the shortest possible time to promote their organization and mutual support, so that human rights and freedom may be won one day, and the number of members in our Union will also increase accordingly. Second, regarding the quality of active members, the original members of our Union (i.e., those belonging to the Commercial Press Office) have already experienced seven years of organizational life. Comparing the actual situation of the seven years of organizational life with the present situation, it can be seen that there has been some improvement. However, our Union fears that they will become complacent after slight improvements in their lives, causing the spirit of solidarity to turn to fatigue, and even causing the organization itself to collapse, the labor-capital contract to disappear without notice, and not realizing the seriousness of the danger. Our Union should strive to revitalize its inherent solidarity and correct its general misconceptions, while also raising its sense of obligation, hoping to achieve progress and enrichment in terms of quality.

Regarding Economic Aspects 223

(1) In addition to continuing to maintain the original labor-capital contract and welfare matters regarding the general treatment of members' work compensation, we will also, to the extent possible, directly seek to further improve working conditions and indirectly reduce the economic burden on members and increase their knowledge and skills by organizing various welfare undertakings. As for newly added members, our Union should first seek their preliminary liberation in the following three areas: (1) raising the current wage to the level of the line and determining the minimum wage; (2) universally implementing an eight-hour workday; (3) improving other working conditions and labor life. Our Union has repeatedly considered that unless the wages of all workers in the industry in the city exceed the level of the line and all working conditions are universally implemented, it is unlikely that workers in the industry will ever reach the realm of coexistence and common prosperity. (2) Attitude towards industrial rationalization: Since the extreme development of international industrial capital organizations, the rationalization movement has been generated accordingly. Countries that follow its abuses have two extremely serious and unsolvable major problems: one is the continuous increase in unemployed workers, and the other is the excessive surplus of commodity production. The continuous increase in unemployed workers is enough to cause a sharp decrease in domestic purchasing power, and the excessive surplus of commodity production is enough to cause the domestic market to be narrow and sluggish. All kinds of symbols are mutually causal. Although its appearance is the embodiment of industrial capital organization and the concentration of wealth, it already harbors the social unrest and shaking that will promote the outbreak of class struggle, reflecting a period of the collapse of international capitalism. It is the inevitable result of the prosperity and decline of international capitalism. The decline of China's industry is inherently due to the fact that backward countries in the international economy are also subject to the constraints of unequal treaties and are regarded by the international community as the only market for selling surplus commodities. At present, the dumping policies of various countries in China are becoming increasingly obvious, which has aroused panic in the domestic industry, and some industrialists and businessmen advocate the implementation of production rationalization in order to increase production efficiency, but they do not take into account the negative effects of rationalization. Such a situation is a major crisis for society. Our Union observes the state of domestic industry and believes that it is not enough to resist international economic aggression without rapidly developing it. However, the strategy for development must be based on the socialization of the means of production and the socialization of commodity distribution, in order to seek the scientification of production technology without harming the physical health of workers, and to make commodities adapt to the supply and demand of society. If we must force the rationalization methods to be applied to the country, cutting our feet to fit the shoes, then there is no one who will not follow the footsteps of international capitalism. For the sake of social peace and the happiness of the people, our Union will devise strict countermeasures to punish those who violate the principles of social people's livelihood.

Regarding Social Aspects 224

Under the capitalist system, our engagement in production work is inherently a condition of being employed by capitalists, but workers in the industry also bear a great responsibility to promote culture and transform society. If we only work to fulfill the conditions of employment, it is tantamount to admitting ourselves to be slaves. Therefore, we must take adapting to the needs of society as the purpose of production, and we must work hard to serve society. Only with the evolution of the entire society can we advance with it.

Regarding Political Aspects 225

To seek the true liberation of the working class, we must wait for the realization of true democratic politics. To seek the realization of true democratic politics, we must first seek the working class to obtain a political position. Because the revolutionary sentiment of the workers is the strongest, the power of their promotion of politics is also the greatest. Politics is driven by revolutionary forces, not only is there no worry about opening the back door, but there is also progress to be expected. That is, our current urgent needs, such as (1) freedom of assembly, association, speech, and publication; (2) the right to strike; (3) the right to vote and participate in government; (4) the right to local self-government; (5) the establishment of all other civil rights, etc., all depend on the working class obtaining a political position before there is an opportunity to implement and realize them. Then the people of all classes may enjoy equal political power in politics, and the embryo of true democratic politics may be formed and even fully established to achieve consolidation. This is not only what the workers in this industry hope for, but also what the workers in all industries in the city and the country are trying to achieve. Therefore, what we want to achieve a political position for is the masses, not for private individuals. Violating this principle is all hypocrisy. Departing from this spirit, even if we run and shout, we can only do our best to shout and have no benefit to the actual benefit.

In summary, in order to achieve each and every one of them, we must make the greatest sacrifices and efforts. As the saying goes, "How can you get tiger cubs without entering the tiger's den?" The people of this Association are ashamed of their lack of strength and heavy responsibilities, and are willing to encourage each other with all the workers in this industry in the city. This is a statement of intent. April 23, 1920

Cotton Cloth Returns to Transport, Customs Workers to Resume Work Today 226

Cotton Cloth Association Refuses to Pay Inspection Fees and Wharf Dues

And Plans to Organize a Transportation Trust Limited Company

The customs workers in this city went on strike. Yesterday, the union issued a notice ordering work to resume this morning. Businessmen were rushing to load goods for export, totaling more than 6,000 pieces. The details are recorded below:

Resumption of Work Notice 227

The Customs Industry Union yesterday notified all members to obey the order to resume work this morning. Regarding the matter of the notice, the Municipal Social Training Order and the attached tripartite agreement were issued, ordering the union to inform the workers to resume work first, etc. Upon receiving this, a general assembly was convened at 7 p.m. yesterday (25th) to discuss the results. This notice will be published as follows: (1) Obey the government's order to resume work on Monday (27th). However, if the Cotton Cloth Association causes further complications or violates the tripartite agreement, it will be dealt with by a second strike. (2) Before a formal treaty is established, temporary accommodations will be made for the delivery of goods from our store and our warehouse. (3) Except for the Lihe Warehouse, all the union drivers in Huishan, Warehouse, Osaka, Huangpu, and Suzhou River will pick up cars at the Bund on Er Ma Road every day from 1:00 p.m.

Strike Losses 228

There are more than 340 cotton cloth companies in the Cotton Cloth Association that sell cotton cloth from the local factories (i.e., white goods), more than 80 such as Hong Shengyuan, more than 100 foreign-style goods such as Tongqing, more than 100 Western-style goods such as Bao Tai, and more than 50 dismantling houses (i.e., door shops) such as Ri Xin Sheng. This time, due to the cartage fee issue for local factory cotton cloth, a labor strike occurred, and foreign goods were affected. Although the customs workers have scheduled to resume transport today, the losses suffered by various companies due to the strike are substantial. There are more than 50 customs agents such as Yuanfeng and Kunji that transport cotton cloth. During the suspension period, about 2,000 pieces were transported for export by foreign customs companies such as Asia, resulting in a loss of about 3-4,000 yuan. After the Customs Workers' Union announced the strike, the various expenses totaled about 1,500 yuan.

Cargo Transportation Resumes 229

After the customs workers decided to resume work uniformly starting today, more than 50 customs agents in this city, such as Merchants Bureau and Yu, dispatched staff members to various customer houses starting yesterday to collect dispatch orders and contact transportation matters. The ships that mainly transport cotton cloth, both Western and local factories, such as the Changjiang Gang, Merchants Bureau's Jiangshun Wheel, Taikoo Company's Shengjing Wheel, Suiding Wheel, Jardine Matheson Company's Lianhe Wheel, Merchants Bureau's Yu Manager Changfeng Wheel, Wentiaban Lian'an Company's Zhoushan Wheel, Beiyangban Taikoo Company's Shuntian Wheel, Daming Wheel, Qingdaoban Taikoo Company's Suzhou Wheel, and Niuzhuangban Zhaoxing Company's Lianxing Wheel, are all scheduled to sail today for export. The Changjiang Gang has about 4,000 pieces of cotton cloth, the Northern Gang has about 1,000 pieces, and the Wentai and other gangs have about 1,000 pieces, totaling more than 6,000 pieces.

Reporting to the Authorities 230

The Customs Industry Union yesterday submitted a document to the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, stating, "The purpose of this document is to inform you that all workers have obeyed your bureau's instructions and have resumed all cotton cloth operations on the 27th of this month. The text is presented for your review. We respectfully received your bureau's Order No. 2941, which stated (omitted). Therefore, we immediately convened a general meeting of all members to discuss the resumption of work. All members agreed that this labor unrest has lasted for two weeks and that we are grateful for your bureau's repeated impartial mediation to resolve this labor unrest. We have decided to resume work on Monday, the 27th of this month, and have decided that if the Cotton Cloth Association causes further complications or does not comply with the tripartite agreement, the workers are prepared to deal with it by a second strike. Therefore, we also ask your bureau to convene the Cotton Cloth Association and the capital's industry association as soon as possible to sign a formal treaty so that an early result can be obtained. This document is specially prepared and submitted for your bureau's review. It is a public convenience. Respectfully presented. At the same time, it has also been reported to the Municipal Party Department and the Civil Training Council."

Association General Assembly 231

The Cotton Cloth Association held a general meeting of members at 2:00 p.m. yesterday. 181 companies such as Ri Xin Sheng Xu Xianglin, Lai Da Chen Songyuan, and Bao Tai Xu Junmo attended. Chairman Chen Songyuan reported on the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau's past mediations and the repeated contacts with the Customs Union, and read out the draft convention previously drafted by the association and the amendments and compromises made by the authorities for discussion and resolution by the public. (1) The origin of the convention should be incorporated. (2) The first article of the amendment agreement was passed. (3) The second article should be fought for by the attending representatives based on the original plan passed by the last general meeting. (4) The third article was passed, but the cotton cloth cartage should be specified as 1.90 cents for double bags and 0.9 cents for single bags. (5) The fourth article should be amended to state that the boundary is north to the Suzhou River and south to the French Concession's Avenue Edward VII. The goods of each shop should be delivered according to the order, and no cartage should be given to banks and warehouses outside the boundary. (6) The words "Western and foreign goods and local factory cotton cloth" in the agreement should be amended to "Various Western and foreign goods, various fabrics, and various local factory cotton cloths." (7) The fifth article was passed. (8) Inspection fees, stamp taxes, and wharf dues were unanimously rejected. (9) Cartage should be paid according to the regulations and should not be increased. Finally, the majority of companies proposed that if the Customs Union does not allow wharf dues and inspection fees, it will organize its own Cotton Cloth Industry Transportation Trust Limited Company. After the chairman repeatedly dissuaded, the proposal was not passed.

Two Silk Industry Unions Send Letters Requesting Employers to Restore Wages

Letter from the Yinxiang District Labor Union 232

The Yinxiang District Silk Filature Workers' Union yesterday sent a letter to the Silk Factory Owners' Association, which stated: "Respectfully, we would like to inform you that in November of last year, the workers, in the spirit of labor-management cooperation and for the sake of the factory's business, painfully agreed to temporarily calculate wages at 85% of the original amount. The suffering endured by the workers in the past half-year is beyond description, which we believe your association is also aware of. On March 13th of this year, at the inaugural meeting of our union, representatives of the members, considering that the original wage rate in Shanghai, where prices are soaring for all goods, was already barely sufficient to maintain the workers' livelihood, let alone at 85% of the original amount, which was even more unsustainable, submitted a proposal to the meeting for discussion. It was resolved to request the factory owners to immediately restore the original wage rate. Upon receiving the resolution from the meeting, our union hoped that commodity prices would fall slightly to ease the burden on the workers, so we did not immediately make a request to your association. However, recently, the price of gold has continued to rise, and commodity prices have followed suit, causing the cost of living to continue to rise uncontrollably. In recent days, workers have come to the union to express their grievances and demand that the factory owners immediately restore the original wage rate, often with tears in their eyes. This situation, this scene, if seen by the factory owners, would also cause them heartache, because the workers' livelihoods are already on the brink of despair. This matter was submitted to the eighth regular meeting of our union yesterday for discussion. All agreed that the workers' livelihood is so dire that restoring the original wage rate is urgently needed. Moreover, since the factory's business was poor last year, the workers were able to painfully understand and forgive the factory owners first. Now that the workers are in distress, the factory owners should not turn a blind eye and fail to fulfill their duty of assistance. Furthermore, it must be understood that wages that are too low will make it impossible for workers to maintain their livelihoods, inevitably leading to a loss of their enthusiasm for work and making it difficult for them to concentrate on their jobs. Then, it will be difficult for the factory owners to ask the workers to work hard to improve production. Therefore, it was resolved to send a letter to your association, requesting you to immediately notify all factories to restore wages to their original level from May 1st, so that workers can maintain their livelihoods and devote themselves to improving production, so that the silk industry can have hope of development, which would benefit not only our labor and management, but also the entire country. We hereby send this letter, hoping that you will immediately comply to alleviate the workers' difficulties and avoid disputes, and please reply within three days. Sincerely, Yinxiang District Silk Filature Workers' Union, April 25th."

Letter from the Zhabei District Labor Union 233

The Zhabei District Silk Filature Workers' Union yesterday sent a letter to the Silk Factory Owners' Association, which stated: "Respectfully, we would like to inform you that in November of last year, our silk filature workers, in view of the sluggish silk market and the difficult business operations of the factories, and in accordance with the principle of labor-management mutual assistance and understanding to seek the development of industry, spared no pain and sacrifice to temporarily calculate wages at 85% of the original amount. This small amount of sincerity was truly for the sake of the factory's business. However, since the wage reduction, the cost of living has not only been difficult to lower, but the price of gold and silver has increased sharply, to the point where the wages of workers who toil all day long are not enough to provide for their own food and clothing, let alone the livelihood of their families. It is pitiful and lamentable. It is no wonder that the labor unrest at the beginning of the month erupted suddenly. When the labor unrest occurred, our union, for the sake of labor-management cooperation and local security, did its utmost to persuade the workers to return to work, and fortunately, it did not spread and expand, and the effort was successful in less than two days. At that time, the reason why our union did not make a request was that we originally believed that the factory owners would be able to realize this and automatically restore the original wage rate. However, we have not seen your understanding. In the past month, not only have the factory owners shown no intention of restoring the wages, but your esteemed association, which upholds justice and seeks the overall development of the silk industry, has also turned a deaf ear. Is this the proper attitude for labor-management cooperation? Moreover, you have deeply failed the workers' original understanding and forgiveness of the factory owners last year.

Page 14

In recent days, workers have come to the union to weep and complain about the pressures of life, one after another. Not only are we in the union heartbroken to witness this, but we believe that your association is also unbearable to hear about it. Therefore, our union held an emergency meeting and resolved to send a letter to your association, requesting you to immediately notify all factories to implement the restoration of the original wage rate from May 1st, in order to prolong the workers' remaining lives and maintain labor-management relations, and to jointly promote the development of the silk industry. If you delay this matter under any pretext and cause unexpected disturbances, your association will be responsible. We hereby send this letter, hoping that you will investigate and handle it, and please reply within three days. Zhabei District Silk Filature Workers' Union."

Refund Method for Shanghai Yarn and Cloth Transported and Sold in Sichuan Province 235

Request from the Yarn Mill Association

Tax Receipts from Yichang to be Used as Verification

The Chinese Yarn Mill Association sent a letter to the General Taxation Office yesterday regarding the refund method for cotton yarn and cloth transported and sold in Sichuan Province. It stated: "Most of the cotton yarn and cloth transported from Shanghai to Sichuan are transshipped via Yichang to Chongqing. Currently, no customs duties are paid for transporting goods from Shanghai to Yichang. However, customs duties must be declared and paid from Yichang to Chongqing. This customs duty should be refunded. Merchants can pay taxes in Yichang, then send the Yichang tax receipt and the duplicate bill of lading back to your office for verification. The already-paid consolidated tax will then be fully refunded to simplify procedures. If approved, please reply so that we can inform the relevant parties."

Recent Continued Reports on the Shaanxi Relief Efforts of the Jisheng Society 236

The Chinese Jisheng Society previously received a report from its relief worker, Mr. Li Yunmen, detailing the situation of the Shaanxi relief efforts, which was published in a previous report. Now, we have received a follow-up report: (1) The relief workers and the burial team set off together on the 5th of this month to investigate and distribute relief in Zhenyuan Town, which was the most severely affected by the disaster. In one day, they investigated and distributed relief in five villages. There were more than thirty corpses in the villages. It is conceivable that there are many corpses in the town, which has about one hundred and ten villages. (2) Distribute seeds for emergency relief to facilitate replanting for the autumn harvest. After the investigation and relief distribution in Zhenyuan Town, relief was distributed in ten towns, including Weigong Town, in four batches and in an orderly manner. Of the third batch of 20,000 yuan in relief funds, 18,000 yuan were received by the Shanghai Tai Chang Fu Qingtai Silver Shop, and 2,000 yuan were received by the De Xingcheng Public Warehouse in the Tianhe Public Warehouse. Verdict on a Collision Between Two Vehicles 241

Both Chauffeurs Were at Fault

Ding Baofa, the chauffeur of Ding Runxiang, a wealthy gentleman, was driving car number 990 on the afternoon of the 11th of this month at 3:00 pm, traveling west on Avenue Petain in the French Concession to Route Lafayette. Unexpectedly, car number 6021, driven by Pei Yufang, was traveling south. The two sides failed to avoid each other and collided, both incurring damage. The police arrived to record the numbers and reported to the head of the patrol. The two parties were summoned to the French Court for interrogation the day before yesterday. First, the head of the vehicle affairs office reported the situation. Then, Mr. Tibbek, the lawyer representing Ding Runxiang, stated that the plaintiff, Ding Runxiang's car, was dispatched by the chauffeur Ding Baofa that day to Tangjiawan to pick up the old lady to return home. Unexpectedly, it was hit by Pei Yufang's car at the intersection of Route Lafayette. The old lady sitting in the car was also seriously injured and is currently still in the hospital for treatment. He requested that the public prosecution part be judged first, and the private prosecution part would be pursued after the appraisal in the future. The defendant, Pei Yufang, was also represented by lawyer Fei Xizhen, who stated that on that day, there was a Public Works Bureau truck parked at the corner, so his client did not see the car traveling from east to west. Ding Baofa, who was driving the car, also did not honk the horn to warn. Who is right and who is wrong? He requested a clear investigation. The Chinese and Western officials ruled that Pei Yufang was fined 15 yuan for careless driving and failing to honk the horn, and Ding Baofa was fined 1 yuan for driving without a license and 5 yuan for failing to honk the horn. The private prosecution was allowed to be reserved.

Old Woman Commits Suicide by Swallowing Opium 242

Caused by a Quarrel with Her Second Daughter-in-law

The Anhui old woman Kuai Sun, aged 65, who lived at 9 Xihefeng Road, Wusong, had two sons, Kuai Xianbing and Kuai LaosI, who were both sailors on the HaiLong dredger of the Junpu Bureau. Sun lived with her two daughters-in-law and grandchildren. Although the old woman was over sixty years old, she was stubborn. Whenever her daughters-in-law slightly disobeyed her, they would be insulted and scolded. However, because the daughters-in-law knew of her age, they did not dare to disobey her. Unexpectedly, she quarreled with her second daughter-in-law again the night before last, and secretly bought half a yuan worth of opium and swallowed it secretly. Then she fell asleep. Later, because she was suffering from poisoning and moaning, her family found a remaining opium bubble in her pocket and realized that she had committed suicide by swallowing opium. Her son, Xianbing, etc., sent her to the Wusong Sanatorium and the Seaside Public Hospital for rescue. However, because she was old and her blood was weak, although Dr. Xu Lanting, etc., tried to treat her, the opium poison was completely vomited out, but she could not overcome the poison, and she died yesterday morning. Her sons, etc., purchased clothing and a coffin and had her buried in the afternoon.

Fire in Jiǔmǔdì Yesterday Afternoon 243

Three Houses Destroyed

At 9:30 am yesterday, a fire suddenly broke out in the home of Chaozhou native Shen A'jing, who was in the fruit business at 30 Gaodun Road, Jiǔmǔdì, South City. The fire spread quickly and was uncontrollable. The fire brigades from various districts in the South City rushed to the scene upon hearing the alarm. After a brief interrogation by Director Xu, he immediately prepared a document to submit to the Judicial Section for interrogation.

Trade Association News

Restaurant Industry 248

The Restaurant Trade Association sent a letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, which stated: "We are writing to you because the Business Tax Preparation Office of the Shanghai Municipal Finance Bureau has issued a notice stating that since the business tax is a newly created tax, we should study it carefully at the beginning of its implementation. If the trade associations in this city have any opinions to propose, they must submit them to the Chamber of Commerce representative for collection or send them to the office for discussion within two weeks. If you need the draft proposal mentioned above, please request it from our office." According to the draft business tax rates for this city proposed by the Municipal Finance Bureau as published in the newspaper, the tax rate for the restaurant industry is 5 per mille of the business turnover, which does not comply with the Business Tax Outline promulgated by the Ministry of Finance, which stipulates that the maximum amount of business tax should not exceed 2 per mille. However, the raw materials used by the restaurant industry, such as fish, chicken, meat, oil, rice, noodles, seafood, and groceries, have all been taxed. Our industry only boils them in a pot to provide food and drink, and then charges a business tax of 5 per mille, which is actually a tax on a tax and does not comply with the principle of one item, one tax. We have learned that the business tax was established after the cessation of tariffs to compensate for local finances and should be levied with a reduction in accordance with the principle of one item, one tax, with 1 or 2 per mille as the maximum amount. In terms of the scope of Shanghai, there are special circumstances that are different from other places, and there is a distinction between the Chinese and foreign concessions. Restaurant industry tycoons and wealthy merchants set up banquets mostly in the concessions. The collection of business tax must be carried out simultaneously in both the Chinese and foreign concessions to ensure fairness, otherwise there will be excuses. The association requests that your esteemed association forward this to the financial authorities for discussion. Please pay attention to the following four items for the restaurant industry representatives attending the business tax discussion: (1) In accordance with Article 11 of the Business Tax Principles, when applying for a business license, it must be stamped by the trade association after investigation before it is issued. This will unify the high collection of business tax and avoid omissions. (2) Collect taxes in accordance with the principle of one item, one tax. (3) The raw materials used in the restaurant industry have all been taxed, and should be collected with a reduction of 1 per mille or exempted from tax. (4) The collection of business tax should be carried out simultaneously in the concessions and the Chinese area to avoid partiality. In summary, we earnestly request your esteemed association to review and approve the adoption and forwarding to alleviate the difficulties of merchants and to promote fairness. We would be grateful for your kindness." (Below omitted)

New-Style Laundry Industry 249

The New-Style Laundry Trade Association held a general meeting of representatives at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce at 1:00 pm on the 25th to discuss industry regulations. The representatives braved the rain to participate and were full of enthusiasm. Mr. Sun Mingqi, a representative from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, and Mr. Cao Zhenqing, a representative from the Municipal Party Department's Civil Training Association, attended to provide guidance. The presidium consisted of Luo Zhenglin, Zhi Kun, and Huang Shoucheng, with Sun Xiaozhu as the recorder. The meeting opened as scheduled. After the chairman's report, the discussion of the industry regulations began. The regulations consisted of six chapters with a total of nineteen articles. Each article was passed after three readings. The list of prices for various colors was too extensive to be discussed and was referred to the review committee consisting of Chen Gaofeng, Zhuang Yufa, Cai Youtang, Fan Zhichen, Wu Xuesong, Ding A'fa, Zhao TiYun, Song Baohai, Song RongSheng, Xu Bao Yuan and Xu Jin Lun. Subsequently, the following proposals were discussed: (1) A proposal to submit a request to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to handle business licenses through the trade associations was approved. (2) A proposal on how to express our position on the fact that the MeiLi Company was fined by the Stamp Tax Bureau for failing to affix stamps to the number plates was unanimously denied and a request was submitted to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to negotiate reasonably. (3) The passing of a declaration opposing the French police's shooting and injury of Xin Hai Shan. (4) To prevent unscrupulous members from falsely establishing business names and absconding with customers' clothes to protect the reputation of the industry. It was resolved that new stores must have two guarantors and be approved by the trade association before they can operate. If absconding occurs, the guarantors will be held accountable and permanently expelled from the industry. (5) A request for legal protection for the Minghua Company in Hongkou, which had newly established a brand name and was obstructing business, was resolved to be handled by the trade association after the Social Affairs Bureau approved it. (6) A proposal that all discount coupons issued by various companies must be cancelled after the industry regulations are approved by the higher authorities was approved. Subsequently, the representatives from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and the Civil Training Association gave guidance one after another, and the meeting was adjourned after refreshments.

Local News Two

A Record of Wei Ru Xiang's Guilt in Stealing Intimacy 254

Having an Affair with Maid Bai Tu Zi

Because the Girl Was Under Sixteen Years of Age

Sentenced to One Year of Imprisonment

A maid named Bai Tu, employed by the Fan family at No. 367 Shunde Lane, Zhejiang Road, is seventeen years old and originally from Wumen. Due to poverty, her mother, Gu Zhang, brought her to Shanghai to work as a kitchen maid to earn a living. The girl had a name, but people called her Bai Tu Zi (White Rabbit) because of her fair complexion, and she gladly accepted it, so her real name was forgotten. Bai Tu Zi not only had fair skin, but was also petite and could please others. Her employer had an adopted son named Wei Ru Xiang (also known as Shi Xiang), who was thirty-nine years old and fond of dressing up. Whenever Bai Tu Zi saw him, they would exchange glances. Wei was skilled at seduction, and so they became intimate. On the nineteenth of last month, Bai Tu Zi quit her job and eloped with Wei. They first stayed at the Phoenix Hotel on Tianjin Road, then moved to the Zhongshan Hotel. Her mother found out and reported it to the Laozha Police Station, which sent detectives to arrest the pair of lovebirds. The next morning, they were sent to the Special District Local Court, where Judge Zhou presided over the trial. According to Gu Zhang's complaint, her daughter Bai Tu Zi had been promised to a Zhang family. Now that Wei had defiled her, the Zhang family would not want to marry her. She requested that the defendant pay 600 yuan to settle the matter with the Zhang family so that her daughter could become Wei's wife. Then, Bai Tu Zi said that she met Wei at the Fan family. Her fiancé was a farmer, and she could not bear the field work, so she did not want to marry him and wished to live with Wei forever. Wei Shi Xiang confessed that he had an affair with the girl. According to the police lawyer Ru Bao Yi, Bai Tu Zi's birthday showed that she was not yet sixteen years old. According to the criminal law, sexual intercourse with a girl under sixteen, even with consent, is considered rape and should be punished according to the rape law. However, Gu Zhang intended to marry her daughter to Wei Shi Xiang and pleaded for leniency, even offering to drop the charges. The lawyer Fan Gang defended the defendant. Judge Zhou finally sentenced Wei to one year of imprisonment for enticing and having sexual intercourse with a girl under twenty years of age. The part of the charge concerning rape was dismissed.

A Lawsuit Involving a Brothel Patron 255

The Brothel Accuses Him of Enticement, Incitement, and Theft

The Patron Accuses Them of False Accusation and Forcing Prostitution for Profit

Cheng Zhangcai, an employee of the electric power company from Nanhui County, recently caused a dispute by arranging for Jin Yuan, a prostitute from the Jicheng brothel in Minhe Lane, Zhejiang Road, to leave the brothel. The two parties sued each other in the Special District Local Court. According to Yang Jicheng, also known as Wang Laoda, Jin Yuan is the biological daughter of Zhu He, a woman living in the city. She is thirty-nine years old. According to the complaint of Lu Qi, the lawyer representing Jicheng, Zhu He, due to poverty, hired Jin Yuan to work as a singer in the Jicheng brothel for a term of four years through a guarantor named Zhang in June of last year. She first gave the brothel an earnest money of 400 yuan, and then used the interest on that amount as Jin Yuan's salary. Jicheng hired a teacher to teach Jin Yuan songs and provided her with clothing, which cost a lot of money. Fortunately, she learned the skills and was able to serve customers. However, Cheng Zhangcai, claiming to be a romantic, saw that Jin Yuan was young and beautiful and used his means to take Jin Yuan out on a car on the second day of the first month of the New Year. They went out to worship the god of joy in the afternoon and did not return until late at night. The maid A Genmei and the old woman were sent to search for them and found them at the Zhu Shunxing Iron Shop in the city, embracing on her mother Zhu He's bed. A Genmei and others knew that Zhu He was not in the room and realized that they could not persuade her to return to the brothel, so they reported back to Jicheng and followed her. Cheng and Jin Yuan had already disappeared. According to Zhu He, Cheng had sent Jin Yuan back, but her whereabouts were still unknown the next day. They invited Zhu He's second daughter and the maid to go to Cheng Zhangcai's residence at No. 1027 Wuzhou Road and found Cheng and Jin Yuan lying in bed in broad daylight. They were awakened by her mother and returned to the brothel. Unexpectedly, the next morning, Jin Yuan took the opportunity to steal gold and pearl bracelets, diamond rings, velvet cloaks, and wool serge cheongsams and disappeared. Jicheng was afraid that this matter would be publicized and would not only affect Jin Yuan's reputation but also hinder business, so she secretly investigated. Unexpectedly, Cheng Zhangcai took the initiative to instruct Jin Yuan to entrust lawyer Lin Yingqing to send a letter to Jicheng claiming that she had broken off relations with him and falsely claiming that the 400 yuan earnest money had been returned in full. Jin Yuan is under twenty years old and her ability to act is still lacking. This incident was purely the result of Cheng Zhangcai colluding with her mother to entice her into having sexual intercourse and inciting her to steal clothing. Therefore, she asked the court to summon the defendants to court and punish Cheng Zhangcai for violating Article 257, Paragraph 2, and Article 337 of the criminal law, and to punish Zhu He for violating Articles 258 and 337 and order them to return the 400 yuan earnest money and clothing. In addition to being represented by lawyer Lin Yingqing, the two defendants also filed a lawsuit against Jicheng for false accusation, claiming that Zhu Jinyuan had been repeatedly abused and forced to receive customers since she was hired by Yang Jicheng. Jinyuan was determined to escape the brothel and borrowed 480 yuan from Cheng Zhangcai. Yang agreed to allow her to redeem herself, but after receiving the money, she went back on her word and harassed her in every way, demanding more than double the original deposit. She also filed a false accusation with the authorities. They asked the court to reject her complaint and to prosecute Yang Jicheng for false accusation, forcing prostitution for profit, and extorting money. The case was originally scheduled to be heard the day before yesterday afternoon. Both parties and witnesses were present as scheduled. However, because Judge Ge was busy hearing other cases, this case could not be heard in detail. He only briefly questioned them and ordered them to be rescheduled for further hearing and investigation.

The Bureau of Public Works Has Established a Special Group to Investigate and Ban Narcotic Substances 256

The West Patrol Head of the Traffic Department is Transferred to Handle the Matter

The Police Department of the Bureau of Public Works has been very serious in investigating and banning opium and cracking down on the private sale of various narcotic drugs in recent years. It originally intended to set up a special office early and select competent staff to be responsible for handling it. However, because the affairs of the Traffic Department were not very busy and it had enough time to take care of both, the establishment of a special office was delayed. The Traffic Department has been handling it until now, and the results are quite considerable, so there seems to be no need to change it. However, the transportation business in the Public Concession is becoming more and more prosperous and complex. The Chinese and foreign staff of the Traffic Department are each performing their duties and still feel that they are too busy to handle other matters. Moreover, the anti-smoking policy is now being vigorously implemented. If special personnel are not set up, it may be difficult to eliminate the poisonous atmosphere. Therefore, the Police Commissioner has set up a group to investigate and ban narcotic substances. All cases of opium and other prohibited items will be handled by this group. The West Patrol Head of the Traffic Department, Mr. Pan Gensi, will be transferred to handle the matter in order to make use of his expertise. Pan's vacancy will be filled by a person with traffic knowledge and experience. The personnel assisting Mr. Pan have also been appointed by the Police Commissioner as West Detective Pu Pu and Chinese Detective Song Bingzheng, detectives Zhang Shaoqing and Ding Yugao. They officially started working on the 21st of this month. From now on, there will be a special person responsible for banning smoking in the concession, which will be more appropriate and may be good news for the future of smoking ban.

Major Reform of Electricity in Wusong 257

Baoming Stops Generating Electricity

Effective May 1st

Wusong Electric Lights has always only had night electricity. Since the completion of the Yin Xing New Power Plant of the Zhabei Water and Electricity Company, the Wusong Baoming Electric Light Company has contacted it to purchase electricity from nearby to feed Wusong. After several negotiations between the two parties, a formal contract was signed in October of last year. Baoming Company immediately laid another main line along Jungong Road and purchased land at the corner of Zhanghuabang Railway West Jungong Road to build an electrical room to install transformers, meters, and main switches. It also laid separate street light lines on various roads in Songzhen to prepare for sending daytime electricity. The street lights can be turned on and off on time. The above project was completed the day before yesterday. It is scheduled to stop generating electricity at the Baoming Power Plant on May 1st and implement the uninterrupted transmission of electricity from the Zhabei New Power Plant day and night. Then, the plant will use transformers to convert high voltage to low voltage for distribution. In the future, Wusong Baoming's general users can have electricity day and night, which will be much more convenient than before.

Sunny Weather Yesterday Attracted Double the Number of Visitors

Longhua Temple in the southwest of Shanghai is a famous ancient temple in Shanghai. Every spring, when the peach blossoms are red and the willows are green, and the vegetables are yellow and the wheat is budding, people bring their families to visit, almost like on the Shanyin Road. Since the beginning of this year, it is a pity that the weather has not been good, with dark clouds and storms from time to time, which has dampened the scenery and caused tourists to stay at home. Yesterday happened to be a sunny Sunday with a gentle breeze, so the number of people from Shanghai who went to sightsee was endless. At 2 p.m., the temple grounds were even more crowded. The No. 2 special buses of the South Shanghai Public Bus also ran extra shifts to facilitate transportation, so tourists praised the convenience.

The Case of the Murder of the Accountant Still Needs Investigation 260

Xu Kuijun, the accountant of the Wuhua Road Refinery in Hongkou, was robbed and hacked to death with a chaotic axe on the evening of January 3 of this year, and more than 7,000 yuan in banknotes were robbed. Afterwards, the Public Security Bureau found that Shi Ruiqing, an apprentice of the factory, and Zhou Awu, a tea room attendant, colluded with bandits from outside to plot to kill the accountant. Shi and Zhou were immediately arrested, and 1,700 yuan in stolen money and bloodstained clothes, a bag, and a sharp axe were found. It was found that the clothes, bag, and sharp axe belonged to Zhou Awu. The axe was the murder weapon. The interrogation revealed that they had confessed and been sent to the Local Court for investigation. The prosecution was clear and filed a public prosecution for robbery and murder. The day before yesterday, Judge Wu opened the trial. Shi Ruiqing confessed that a total of eight people came in, stayed in the inner accounting room for two hours, took the banknotes, and divided them at the outer accounting counter. I was monitored and did not participate in anything. After they were divided, they ordered me to go to sleep. At that time, Zhou Awu was holding the axe and also came out of the inner accounting room. Zhou Awu gave me 1,700 yuan at dawn to keep for him, saying that he was afraid that things would be leaked and threatened not to report, otherwise he would kill me. Later, my senior brother called me out to play, but I was arrested. Zhou Awu confessed that he was sleeping in the kitchen room with four other people. I only know one name, Fusheng. The accountant was killed while I was sleeping and I didn't know anything about it, and I didn't send any money to Shi Ruiqing. When asked how there was blood on his clothes, he replied that it was from his hands cracking open from the cold. When asked where the blood on the package came from, he replied that he didn't know. When asked why he didn't call Mr. Xu when he went to the accounting room the next morning, but called Mr. Ye, did you know that Xu was dead? He replied that this was not the case. I called Mr. Xu because the silver boxes were opened and I went to the bedroom with the student Chen Kangnian and saw that he had been hacked to death. The apprentice Chen Kangnian said that I lived with Shi Ruiqing. When the incident happened, I was already asleep. The next morning, I went in first and saw that the silver box was open. Later, Zhou Awu came and said he was going to call Mr. Ye. I said to call Mr. Xu, so we went to Mr. Xu's place and saw that he was dead. Xu Lanfang, the son of the deceased, said that his father was kind and had no enemies. He had a good relationship with his colleagues in the factory. I don't know the reason for his death this time. The interrogating official believed that the case still needed investigation, so he ordered it to be rescheduled for trial and the defendant was remanded in custody.

Firearms Hidden in a Bamboo Box with a False Bottom 263

Tian Zhengxin, a police officer of the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau's water patrol team, was patrolling the river to the Dada Wharf at about 1 a.m. yesterday when he saw the Dade steamer berthed there and had not yet set sail. He immediately boarded the ship to conduct an inspection. He found a bamboo box and a net basket at the stern of the ship, but no one was guarding them. When he inquired about the owner of the items, a man came forward and claimed to be Gu Rongji and admitted that the box and basket were his. He immediately tried to open the bamboo box and search it. He found three pancakes and blue cloth short shirts and trousers, but no prohibited items. When he turned over the bottom of the box, he found that the bottom was made of wood, but the outside was made of bamboo. He immediately became suspicious and pried open the wooden bottom of the box. He found that the box had a false bottom and contained thirteen rifle springs, eight barrels, three bolts, and fourteen parts needed for the gun. Then, he found three rifle springs, four barrels, one bolt, and orange peel tea in the net basket. He brought the witnesses back to the team. When Chief Xu of the General Team interrogated Gu Yueji, he confessed that he was 58 years old and from Funing. This time, I took the steamer to Jiangbei because of something. On the ship, I met a fellow villager who I didn't know who asked me to take care of the box and basket for him. He went to look for a room elsewhere. I really didn't know there were prohibited items hidden inside and I was deceived. I asked for your understanding. He was ordered to submit a document to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for questioning.

The Stolen Coffins Are Mostly Those of Women

After the Theft, the Female Genitals Are Often Incomplete

Unexpectedly, the coffin of a Huang woman from Wusong was also stolen, and the coffin of a Zhao woman from Baoshan was also stolen in the same area. A Young Girl Escapes Before Her Wedding 268

It Turns Out She Was Abducted and Hidden by a Militia Member

The second team of the Pengpu Security Corps in Zhabei suddenly received a report from the plaintiff Zhang Qichang at about 9 p.m. the night before last (the 25th) that Yang Yufu, a militia member who had been dismissed by the team, reported that he was 23 years old, from Yangzhou, and lived at No. 80 Pushan Road. He made ribbons for a living. He had a younger sister named Xiaolan, who was 18 years old and had been promised to a son of the Sheng family in her hometown. On the 15th of this month, my father, Dingjiu, sent Xiaolan home to get married. Unexpectedly, Xiaolan suddenly disappeared when the Yangzhou ship docked at the pier. I immediately searched everywhere without success. The people and Yang Yufu are neighbors, and Xiaolan and Yang's wife are very close and travel back and forth very often. Moreover, Yang Yufu also went to Yangzhou three days after Xiaolan left, which is obviously very suspicious. For this reason, he was arrested and sent to the team for interrogation. According to Yang Yufu's confession, my adoptive father Gao Songchao opened a pancake shop in Yangzhou. Recently, he became seriously ill and sent a letter requesting money and urging me to go to Yangzhou. Because I went to Yangzhou to visit him the day before, I didn't know anything about Zhang Xiaolan's escape. The team verified the confession and believed that the case involved abduction and the confessions of both parties were different, so they sentenced him to the Shanghai Local Court for trial. After the team's Pushan Road substation squad leader Qiao Huaqing inquired further, Yang Yufu's wife revealed the truth, saying that Xiaolan was indeed abducted and hidden by her husband and has now been brought back from Yangzhou and hidden in a certain place in Pudong. After hearing this, Squad Leader Qiao immediately reported to the team headquarters and led plainclothes officers to investigate and found Xiaolan and arrested her. According to Xiaolan's confession to the Third District Public Security Bureau, she and Yang Yufu took a boat to Zhenjiang, transferred to a fourth-class car to Shanghai, stayed in an inn for two nights, and then sent her to Yang's friend's place for only one night. Xiaolan is currently being held in the district because it is Sunday and will be transferred to the Shanghai Local Court for trial tomorrow.

Pirates Rob Fishing Boats Again 269

Since this spring, pirates have been rampant on the waters of Daji Mountain outside Wusongkou. In recent months, fishing boats carrying goods have been robbed of silver dollars by pirates, or the crew members have been kidnapped and held for ransom, which has caused fishing boats to not dare to transport them, so they have asked the Fishery Association to petition the water police to strictly suppress them and send police ships to patrol and protect them in the waters. Now is the fishing season, and the fishing boats going back and forth to the market are even more prosperous. If they are not suppressed, the navigation is worrisome, so the association has petitioned the water police district to strictly suppress them to secure the shipping merchants. At the moment, the water police are suppressing them and have ordered patrol boats to patrol the waters and informed the fishing boats to carry out transportation as usual. However, on the 20th of this month, the Zheng Zhangsheng fishing boat was fully loaded with fresh yellow croaker in Ningbo and was transporting it to Shanghai for sale. Unexpectedly, when it sailed to the south entrance of Daji Mountain, it encountered a large group of pirates sailing in more than a dozen small boats. They fired their guns and ordered them to stop. A helmsman was shot and killed and the boat was also shot with holes. When Zheng's boat stopped, dozens of pirates swarmed onto the boat, all speaking with a Taizhou accent and threatening them with guns to prevent them from making a sound. The pirates searched everywhere and only found more than 200 yuan, which made them very angry. The pirates dragged a group of people out and asked where the shipowner was. The group did not understand the Taizhou language, so they could not answer. The pirates randomly slashed at them. The shipowner Zheng heard the sound and came out, and the pirates beat him and forced him to hand over the silver dollars. When they failed, they kidnapped him and left. When they left, they said to the crew members to prepare 2,000 yuan to redeem the shipowner. After the pirates left, Zheng's boat sailed to the seaside of Chuansha and borrowed money from other boats to buy a coffin to collect the helmsman and send the injured crew members to the hospital for treatment. Yesterday, the crew members came to Shanghai to report to the fish market that the boat had been shot with holes and had to be repaired before it could sail, so the market hired a boat to transport and sell the goods from Zheng's boat and petitioned the water police to arrest the pirates.

The Datong Bookstore's main store on Fourth Horse Road has been very prosperous since it moved to its new location at the Wangping Street entrance. It is scheduled to officially open today and hold a 15th anniversary commemorative discount for 35 days. In addition to practical discounts, a gift will be given for every 30 cents of books purchased. For example, if you purchase one yuan, you can get an ivory seal with a stone-carved character. If you purchase five yuan, you can get a five-yuan savings certificate from the Anhui Bank. All are reduced for customers, which is a grand event in the publishing industry.
